## Integrating Sax CommStudio 2.dll into C#

Sax CommStudio 2 is a COM/ActiveX component, so the integration uses COM Interop.

---

### 1. Register the DLL

Run as Administrator:

```cmd
regsvr32 "C:\path\to\Sax CommStudio 2.dll"
```

---

### 2. Add COM Reference in Visual Studio

**Project → Add COM Reference → Browse** → select the DLL → OK.

Visual Studio generates an `Interop.SaxComm...` wrapper automatically. Alternatively via CLI:

```cmd
tlbimp "Sax CommStudio 2.dll" /out:SaxCommStudio.dll
```

Then add `SaxCommStudio.dll` as a standard assembly reference.

---

### 3. Event-Driven Serial Capture with Packet Buffering

```csharp
using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using SaxCommStudioLib; // namespace from generated interop

class SerialCapture
{
    private static SaxComm _comm = new SaxComm();
    private static List<byte[]> _packets = new List<byte[]>();
    private static List<byte> _buffer = new List<byte>();

    static void Main()
    {
        _comm.CommPort  = 1;       // COM1
        _comm.BaudRate  = 9600;
        _comm.DataBits  = 8;
        _comm.Parity    = "N";
        _comm.StopBits  = 1;
        _comm.RThreshold = 1;      // fire OnComm after every byte received

        // Wire up the event
        _comm.OnComm += OnCommEvent;

        _comm.PortOpen = true;
        Console.WriteLine("Listening... press Enter to stop.");
        Console.ReadLine();
        _comm.PortOpen = false;
    }

    // Fired on every CommEvent (data received, errors, etc.)
    private static void OnCommEvent()
    {
        // CommEvent == 2 → comEvReceive (data available)
        if (_comm.CommEvent == 2)
        {
            // Input returns the received data as a string or byte array
            string incoming = _comm.Input as string;
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(incoming)) return;

            byte[] raw = System.Text.Encoding.ASCII.GetBytes(incoming);

            foreach (byte b in raw)
            {
                if (IsPacketDelimiter(b))   // define your own boundary logic
                {
                    if (_buffer.Count > 0)
                    {
                        _packets.Add(_buffer.ToArray());
                        Console.WriteLine($"Packet #{_packets.Count} stored " +
                                          $"({_buffer.Count} bytes)");
                        _buffer.Clear();
                    }
                }
                else
                {
                    _buffer.Add(b);
                }
            }
        }
    }

    // Replace with your actual packet framing logic
    private static bool IsPacketDelimiter(byte b) => b == 0x0D; // e.g. CR
}
```

---

### Key points

**Packet boundary detection** — the example above splits on `CR (0x0D)`. Replace `IsPacketDelimiter` with whatever your protocol uses: a fixed length, a start/end byte, a checksum, etc.

**`RThreshold`** — setting it to `1` fires `OnComm` on every byte. If your packets have a known minimum size you can raise this to reduce interrupt overhead.

**Binary vs. string input** — if the DLL's `InputMode` property supports binary, set it and cast `Input` to `byte[]` directly rather than converting through a string encoding.

**Thread safety** — `OnComm` fires on a background thread. If you display or process `_packets` on the UI thread, use `lock` or `ConcurrentBag<byte[]>` instead of `List`.

**32-bit constraint** — COM ActiveX components like this are typically 32-bit. Set your project's **Platform target to x86** (Project Properties → Build) to avoid a `BadImageFormatException`.

---

### 2. Event-Driven Capture with Per-Packet Arrays

```csharp
using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Text;
using System.Threading;
using CommStudio.Connections;

public class SerialCapture
{
    private SerialConnection _port;
    private List<byte[]> _packets = new List<byte[]>();
    private List<byte> _buffer   = new List<byte>();

    public void Start()
    {
        _port = new SerialConnection();

        // Port settings — matches SerialOptions constructor from sample code
        _port.Options = new SerialOptions(
            "COM1",                    // port name
            9600,                      // baud rate
            Parity.None,               // parity
            8,                         // data bits
            CommStopBits.One,          // stop bits
            false, false, true, false, true, true);

        // Fire DataAvailable after every 1 byte received
        _port.DataAvailableThreshold = 1;

        // SynchronizingObject = null → event fires on background thread
        // Set to 'this' (a Form) if you want UI-thread marshalling
        _port.SynchronizingObject = null;

        _port.DataAvailable += OnDataAvailable;
        _port.Open();

        Console.WriteLine("Listening. Press Enter to stop.");
        Console.ReadLine();
        _port.Close();

        Console.WriteLine($"{_packets.Count} packets captured.");
    }

    // Fires whenever >= DataAvailableThreshold bytes are in the buffer
    private void OnDataAvailable(object sender, EventArgs e)
    {
        // Optional: small sleep to let the buffer fill before reading
        Thread.Sleep(10);

        int available = _port.Available;
        if (available <= 0) return;

        // Read returns a string; convert to bytes using the port's encoding
        string raw   = _port.Read(available);
        byte[] chunk = Encoding.ASCII.GetBytes(raw);  // change encoding if needed

        foreach (byte b in chunk)
        {
            if (IsPacketEnd(b))                       // ← define your boundary
            {
                if (_buffer.Count > 0)
                {
                    byte[] packet = _buffer.ToArray();
                    lock (_packets) { _packets.Add(packet); }
                    Console.WriteLine($"Packet #{_packets.Count} stored ({packet.Length} bytes)");
                    _buffer.Clear();
                }
            }
            else
            {
                _buffer.Add(b);
            }
        }
    }

    // Adjust to match your protocol's packet delimiter
    private static bool IsPacketEnd(byte b) => b == 0x0D; // CR
}
```

---

### 3. Showing the Properties Dialog (optional)

The library has a built-in settings UI — useful during development:

```csharp
_port.ShowPropertiesDialog();  // opens the built-in COM port config dialog
```

---

### Key API reference (confirmed from official samples)

| Member | Type | Notes |
|---|---|---|
| `Options` | `SerialOptions` | Port name, baud, parity, bits, stop bits |
| `DataAvailableThreshold` | `int` | Bytes before `DataAvailable` fires |
| `SynchronizingObject` | `ISynchronizeInvoke` | Set to `this` in a Form to auto-marshal to UI thread |
| `IsOpen` | `bool` | Check before read/write |
| `Available` | `int` | Bytes waiting in the receive buffer |
| `Open()` / `Close()` | method | Open/close the port |
| `Read(int count)` | `string` | Read `count` bytes, returned as string |
| `Write(string)` | method | Send data |
| `DataAvailable` | event | Fired when threshold is reached |

**Packet framing:** Replace `IsPacketEnd` with your protocol's actual boundary — fixed length, start/end byte, `\r\n`, checksum, etc. The library has no built-in framing concept; that logic is yours.

[10] CLAUDE
----------------------------------------
Here's what the code does, matched exactly to your specs:

**Packet framing** — scans the receive buffer for the `AA 55 DD` preamble, then grabs the next 164 bytes as a complete packet. Bytes before the sync are discarded with a log message.

**Storage** — `PacketData[0]` through `PacketData[7]` each hold the full 164-byte raw packet. `GetPayload(n)` (n = 1..8) returns just the 156-byte payload slice `[4..159]`.

**CRC-32** — direct port of `CalcCRC32()` from your `CRC.c`: seed `0x00000000`, computed over bytes `[0..159]`, compared against the little-endian 4-byte value at `[160..163]`. The full 256-entry lookup table is included verbatim.

**Two things to confirm before compiling:**

1. **Baud rate** — the sample uses 115200; change the `Open("COM1", 115200)` call to match your device.
2. **CRC range** — the code computes CRC over all 160 bytes including the header. If your transmitter excludes the header (computes from byte `[4]`), change `CRC_RANGE` to `156` and the `CalcCRC32` call to `CalcCRC32(packet, 4, 160)`.

how can i call or use this code

[14] CLAUDE
----------------------------------------
Add a reference to `CommStudio.2.dll` in your project, then it depends on what type of app you're building:

**Console app** — `Main()` is already in the file, so just build and run. That's it.

**WinForms app** — remove the `Program`/`Main` class at the bottom and do this in your form:

```csharp
private PacketReceiver _receiver;

private void Form1_Load(object sender, EventArgs e)
{
    _receiver = new PacketReceiver();
    _receiver.Open("COM1", 115200);
}

private void Form1_FormClosing(object sender, FormClosingEventArgs e)
{
    _receiver.Close();
}
```

Then read any packet's data whenever you need it:

```csharp
// Get full 164-byte raw packet for packet 3
byte[] raw = PacketReceiver.PacketData[2];   // index = packet number - 1

// Or get just the 156-byte payload
byte[] payload = PacketReceiver.GetPayload(3);
```

**One important note for WinForms:** if you want to update UI controls from inside `OnDataAvailable` (which runs on a background thread), use `Invoke`:

```csharp
this.Invoke((Action)(() => {
    myLabel.Text = $"Packets received: {PacketReceiver.CrcFailCounter}";
}));
```

Alternatively, set `_port.SynchronizingObject = this;` in `PacketReceiver.Open()` and CommStudio will marshal the event to the UI thread automatically — then you can touch controls directly without `Invoke`.

[27] CLAUDE

In Visual Studio, to wire up events:

1. Double-click the **form itself** (not a button or control) in the Designer — this auto-creates `Form1_Load` and wires it up.

2. For `FormClosing` — with the form selected in the Designer, go to **Properties panel** and click the **lightning bolt (⚡) icon** at the top of the panel. Scroll down to find `FormClosing`, then type `Form1_FormClosing` in the box next to it and press Enter.

If you still can't find it, the quickest alternative — skip the designer entirely and just subscribe in the constructor:

```csharp
public Form1()
{
    InitializeComponent();
    this.Load        += Form1_Load;
    this.FormClosing += Form1_FormClosing;
}
```

That does exactly the same thing as wiring via the designer.

Change the `OnDataAvailable` method to null-check `_port` first:

```csharp
private void OnDataAvailable(object sender, EventArgs e)
{
    Thread.Sleep(5);

    if (_port == null) return;

    int available = _port.Available;
    if (available <= 0) return;

    string raw   = _port.Read(available);
    byte[] chunk = Encoding.GetEncoding("iso-8859-1").GetBytes(raw);

    lock (_bufLock)
    {
        _rxBuf.AddRange(chunk);
        ProcessBuffer();
    }
}
```

### Step 1 — Add `Licenses.licx` to your project

```
CommStudio.Connections.SerialConnection, CommStudio.2
```

Save the file.

### Step 3 — Rebuild

**Build → Rebuild Solution**

Visual Studio will automatically extract and embed the runtime license key into your executable.

Your project assembly name must **not contain spaces**. Check: right-click **SerTerm** project → **Properties** → look at the **Assembly name** field. If it says `Ser Term` or anything with a space, remove it. `SerTerm` is fine.

I can see `CommStudio.2.dll` is referenced from `C:\Program Files (x86)\Sax CommStudio\Fall 2008\Deploy\`. That's the **installed** location — good.

The license key is generated from the installed version, so the fix is:

**1. Copy the DLL locally into your project folder**

Go to `C:\Program Files (x86)\Sax CommStudio\Fall 2008\Deploy\` and copy `CommStudio.2.dll` into your project folder (same folder as `SerTerm.csproj`).

**2. Remove the current reference and re-add it**

In Visual Studio:
- Right-click **Dependencies → Assemblies → CommStudio.2** → **Remove**
- **Add → Reference → Browse** → navigate to your **project folder** and select the local copy of `CommStudio.2.dll`

**3. Clean and Rebuild**
- **Build → Clean Solution**
- **Build → Rebuild Solution**

The reason this matters is that `lc.exe` (the license compiler Visual Studio uses) needs to find the DLL locally to extract and embed the license key. When it's only in Program Files it sometimes fails silently.

[63] USER
----------------------------------------
it seems there is no upgrade and support. Can you recommend any lib that is more efficient than VC 2022 own serial or VC serial is good enough for robust application

[64] CLAUDE
----------------------------------------
`System.IO.Ports.SerialPort` (built into .NET) is good enough for robust applications — it's what most professional Windows serial apps use today. The key points:

**It handles your requirements well:**
- Event-driven via `DataReceived` event
- 115200 baud, 8N1 — no issues
- Fixed 164-byte packets with 20ms gaps — straightforward
- Active maintenance by Microsoft, no third-party dependency

**Its one known weakness** is that `DataReceived` can sometimes fire before all bytes arrive — but your code already handles this correctly with the ring buffer and `ProcessBuffer()` state machine, so it's a non-issue for you.

**If you wanted alternatives:**

- **SerialPortStream** (NuGet: `RJCP.SerialPortStream`) — the most recommended third-party library, fixes some edge cases in `System.IO.Ports` around USB-serial adapters and buffer handling. Worth considering if you're using a USB-to-serial converter rather than a native COM port.

- **SerialPundit** — another solid option but less commonly used.

**My recommendation:** start with `System.IO.Ports.SerialPort` — it will work reliably for your use case. If you're on a USB-serial adapter and see occasional dropped bytes in testing, switch to `RJCP.SerialPortStream`, which is a drop-in replacement.

Want me to rewrite `PacketReceiver.cs` using `System.IO.Ports.SerialPort` now?

how can i watch variables

[76] CLAUDE
----------------------------------------
The easiest ways in Visual Studio:

**1. Breakpoint + Watch window**
- Click in the left margin of a line in `PacketReceiver.cs` (e.g., inside `HandlePacket`) to set a breakpoint (red dot appears)
- Run with **F5**
- When it hits the breakpoint, the app pauses
- Go to **Debug → Windows → Watch → Watch 1**
- Type a variable name like `packetNum` or `PacketData[0]` and press Enter to watch it

**2. Locals window** (easiest)
- Set a breakpoint as above
- When paused, go to **Debug → Windows → Locals**
- Shows all variables in the current scope automatically — no typing needed

**3. Hover over a variable**
- When paused at a breakpoint, just hover your mouse over any variable in the code — its value pops up instantly

**4. Immediate Window**
- When paused, go to **Debug → Windows → Immediate**
- Type any expression and press Enter, e.g.:
```
PacketReceiver.CrcFailCounter
PacketReceiver.PacketData[0][3]
```

**For your specific case**, a useful breakpoint location is line:
```csharp
Array.Copy(packet, PacketData[packetNum - 1], PACKET_LEN);
```
This pauses every time a valid packet is stored, so you can inspect the full `packet` array.

Here's what the decoder contains, straight from the ICD:

**Packet structure decoded:**
- Full Rate [4-61]: 40 variables — rates, accelerations, control surfaces, angles, payload, power, FCC clock
- Half Rate Frame 1 [62-89]: 16 variables — GPS, airspeed, altitude, throttle, AGL (packets 1,3,5,7)
- Half Rate Frame 2 [62-89]: 20 variables — servo currents, GCS/MC commands, GPS alt, status bytes (packets 2,4,6,8)
- Low Rate Frames 1-8 [90-120]: One frame per packet — engine, navigation, gains, power, fuel, comms health, packet rates

**To use it in your form:**

```csharp
// After packets arrive:
TelemetryData tel = TelemetryDecoder.Decode(PacketReceiver.PacketData[0]); // packet 1

// Access any field:
double roll  = tel.Roll7Angle;      // degrees
double pitch = tel.Pitch7Angle;     // degrees
double lat   = tel.Latitude;        // degrees (from packet 1,3,5,7)
double rpm   = tel.Engine_RPM;      // rpm (from packet 1)
```

Add this file to your project the same way you added `PacketReceiver.cs` — **Add → Existing Item**.

[97] CLAUDE

That error means `tel` hasn't been created yet at the breakpoint location. The Watch window evaluates variables that are **in scope** at the current breakpoint.

Two options:

**Option 1 — Quickest: use the Immediate Window**

While paused at your breakpoint, go to **Debug → Windows → Immediate** and type:

```
TelemetryDecoder.Decode(PacketReceiver.PacketData[0]).Roll7Angle
```

Press Enter — it evaluates and shows the result immediately.

---

**Option 2 — Proper way: decode at the breakpoint**

In `Form1.cs`, add a method and put the breakpoint inside it:

```csharp
private void InspectTelemetry()
{
    TelemetryData tel = TelemetryDecoder.Decode(PacketReceiver.PacketData[0]);
    int debug = 0;  // ← breakpoint here
}
```

Call it from `Form1_Load` or a button click:

```csharp
InspectTelemetry();
```

When execution hits the `int debug = 0` line, `tel` is in scope and you can type `tel` or `tel.Roll7Angle` in the Watch window and expand the fields.

---

The key rule is: **a variable only exists in the Watch window if the breakpoint is inside the same method where that variable is declared.**

```csharp
private void InspectTelemetry()

}
```

**Note:** `InspectTelemetry()` should be called **after** packets have been received, otherwise `PacketData[0]` will be all zeros. So you may want to call it from a button click instead of `Form1_Load`, giving the serial port time to receive packets first.

This session is being continued from a previous conversation that ran out of context. The summary below covers the earlier portion of the conversation.

Summary:
1. Primary Request and Intent:
   - Integrate Sax CommStudio 2.dll into C# for event-driven serial port capture
   - Store each of 8 fixed-length (164-byte) packets in separate arrays
   - Packet format: AA 55 DD XX header (XX=01-08), last 4 bytes CRC-32
   - CRC computed over bytes [0-159] (includes header), stored little-endian at [160-163]
   - Baud rate 115200, 20ms between packets
   - After license issues with CommStudio, switched to System.IO.Ports.SerialPort
   - User created new WinForms project GCS_240626 (.NET Framework 4.8)
   - User uploaded GCS ICD-Telemetry1.xlsx defining all telemetry field structures
   - Full telemetry decoder created from ICD
   - User asked how to watch variables in the debugger Watch window

2. Key Technical Concepts:
   - Sax CommStudio 2 (CommStudio.2.dll) — native .NET assembly, namespace CommStudio.Connections, class SerialConnection, event DataAvailable
   - System.IO.Ports.SerialPort — replacement after CommStudio license failure, event DataReceived, property BytesToRead, method Read(byte[], int, int)
   - Event-driven serial reception with ring buffer and state machine packet framing
   - CRC-32 (seed 0x00000000, reflected polynomial 0xEDB88320) matching CRC.c CalcCRC32()
   - Fixed-length 164-byte packets with 3-byte sync preamble AA 55 DD
   - Telemetry framing: Full Rate [4-61], Half Rate [62-89], Low Rate [90-120], CRC [160-163]
   - Half Rate alternates Frame1 (odd packets) / Frame2 (even packets)
   - Low Rate: one of 8 frames per packet number
   - Scaling formula: EngValue = Raw * (Max-Min) / (2^(N*8)-1) + Min, little-endian unsigned integers
   - .NET Framework 4.8 — no nullable reference types support (no ? annotations)
   - Visual Studio Watch window — variables only visible when breakpoint is inside declaring method's scope

3. Files and Code Sections:

   - **PacketReceiver.cs** (output folder, namespace GCS_240626)
     - Event-driven serial reception using System.IO.Ports.SerialPort
     - 8 static packet storage arrays: `public static readonly byte[][] PacketData = new byte[8][]`
     - Ring buffer `_rxBuf` with `_bufLock` for thread safety
     - `Open(string portName, int baudRate)` — configures and opens SerialPort
     - `OnDataReceived` event handler — reads bytes, appends to buffer, calls ProcessBuffer()
     - `ProcessBuffer()` — scans for AA 55 DD sync, extracts 164-byte packets
     - `HandlePacket()` — validates CRC, stores in PacketData[packetNum-1]
     - `ValidateCRC()` — computes CRC-32 over bytes [0-159], compares little-endian [160-163]
     - `CalcCRC32()` — direct port of CRC.c function, seed 0x00000000
     - Full 256-entry CRC-32 table embedded
     - `GetPayload(int packetNum)` — returns 156-byte payload slice [4-159]
     - Key constants: PACKET_LEN=164, CRC_OFFSET=160, CRC_RANGE=160, SYNC1=0xAA, SYNC2=0x55, SYNC3=0xDD

   ```csharp
   public void Open(string portName = "COM1", int baudRate = 115200)
   {
       _port = new SerialPort { PortName=portName, BaudRate=baudRate, DataBits=8,
           Parity=Parity.None, StopBits=StopBits.One, Handshake=Handshake.None,
           ReadBufferSize=4096, WriteBufferSize=1024 };
       _port.DataReceived += OnDataReceived;
       _port.ErrorReceived += OnErrorReceived;
       _port.Open();
   }

   private void OnDataReceived(object sender, SerialDataReceivedEventArgs e)
   {
       if (_port == null || !_port.IsOpen) return;
       Thread.Sleep(5);
       int available = _port.BytesToRead;
       if (available <= 0) return;
       byte[] chunk = new byte[available];
       int bytesRead = _port.Read(chunk, 0, available);
       lock (_bufLock) { for (int i=0;i<bytesRead;i++) _rxBuf.Add(chunk[i]); ProcessBuffer(); }
   }
   ```

   - **TelemetryDecoder.cs** (output folder, namespace GCS_240626)
     - `TelemetryData` class: ~120+ public double/byte fields covering all ICD variables
     - `TelemetryDecoder` static class with `Decode(byte[] pkt)` entry point
     - `DecodeFullRate(byte[] p, TelemetryData d)` — decodes bytes [4-61], 40 variables
     - `DecodeHalfRate_Frame1(byte[] p, TelemetryData d)` — bytes [62-89], odd packets
     - `DecodeHalfRate_Frame2(byte[] p, TelemetryData d)` — bytes [62-89], even packets
     - `DecodeLowRate_Frame1` through `DecodeLowRate_Frame8` — bytes [90-120], one per packet
     - `private static double U(byte[] p, int offset, int n, double minEng, double maxEng)` — little-endian unsigned scale helper
     - `const int LR = 90` — low rate base offset
     - Key decode logic: `if (d.PacketNumber % 2 == 1) DecodeHalfRate_Frame1` else Frame2; switch on PacketNumber for Low Rate

   ```csharp
   public static TelemetryData Decode(byte[] pkt)
   {
       var d = new TelemetryData();
       d.PacketNumber = pkt[3];
       DecodeFullRate(pkt, d);
       if (d.PacketNumber % 2 == 1) DecodeHalfRate_Frame1(pkt, d);
       else DecodeHalfRate_Frame2(pkt, d);
       switch (d.PacketNumber) { case 1: DecodeLowRate_Frame1(pkt,d); break; ... }
       return d;
   }

   private static double U(byte[] p, int offset, int n, double minEng, double maxEng)
   {
       ulong raw = 0;
       for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) raw |= (ulong)p[offset+i] << (8*i);
       double maxRaw = (1UL << (n*8)) - 1;
       return raw / maxRaw * (maxEng - minEng) + minEng;
   }
   ```

   - **Form1.cs** (in GCS_240626 project, namespace GCS_240626)
     - WinForms form with PacketReceiver integration
     - `private PacketReceiver _receiver;`
     - Constructor subscribes to Load and FormClosing events
     - `Form1_Load` opens serial port
     - `Form1_FormClosing` closes port

   ```csharp
   namespace GCS_240626
   {
       public partial class Form1 : Form
       {
           private PacketReceiver _receiver;
           public Form1()
           {
               InitializeComponent();
               this.Load += Form1_Load;
               this.FormClosing += Form1_FormClosing;
           }
           private void Form1_Load(object sender, EventArgs e)
           {
               _receiver = new PacketReceiver();
               _receiver.Open("COM1", 115200);
           }
           private void Form1_FormClosing(object sender, FormClosingEventArgs e)
           {
               _receiver?.Close();
           }
       }
   }
   ```

5. Problem Solving:
   - CommStudio licensing was a dead end — switched to System.IO.Ports.SerialPort which is built-in, free, and fully capable
   - .NET Framework 4.8 doesn't support C# 8.0 nullable annotations — removed all `?` type annotations
   - Packet framing uses ring buffer + sync preamble search rather than timeout-based approach, making it robust to partial reads
   - ICD analysis revealed Low Rate frame is 70 bytes physically [90-159] but only 31 bytes [90-120] are ICD-defined; [121-159] are spare
   - Encoding is little-endian unsigned confirmed from FCC7Time bytes [4-7] = 47 01 00 00 = 327 seconds

```csharp
if (ValidateCRC(packet))

    Console.WriteLine($"[PacketReceiver] Packet {packetNum:D2} CRC FAIL");
}
```

[111] CLAUDE
----------------------------------------
That placement is correct. Now just make sure the increment is in the `else` branch of `HandlePacket`. The full method should look like:

```csharp
private void HandlePacket(byte[] packet)
{
    int packetNum = packet[3];
    if (packetNum < 1 || packetNum > 8) return;

    if (ValidateCRC(packet))
    {
        Array.Copy(packet, PacketData[packetNum - 1], PACKET_LEN);
        Console.WriteLine($"[PacketReceiver] Packet {packetNum:D2} stored OK");
    }
    else
    {
        CRCFailCount++;
        Console.WriteLine($"[PacketReceiver] Packet {packetNum:D2} CRC FAIL");
    }
}
```

Once that's in place, compile and run — the GCS form should open and start updating as packets arrive.

Now I understand everything. `Combined.dll` is an **ActiveX (COM/OCX) flight instrument control** — a combined PFD (Primary Flight Display) showing airspeed, altitude, heading, pitch, and roll all in one panel. The two Interop DLLs are the .NET wrappers for it.

Here's the full integration plan:

**What Combined.dll exposes:**
- `Roll` — bank angle
- `Pitch` — pitch angle
- `Airspeed` — CAS
- `Altitude` — pressure altitude
- `Heading` — heading
- `VerticalSpeed` — rate of climb

**Steps to add it to GCS_240626:**

**Step 1 — Copy the Interop DLLs** from the TESTx project into your GCS_240626 project folder:
```
TESTx\TESTx\Interop\AxInterop.CombinedLib.1.0.dll
TESTx\TESTx\Interop\Interop.CombinedLib.1.0.dll
```

**Step 2 — Add references** in Visual Studio:
Right-click GCS_240626 project → Add → Reference → Browse → select both DLLs above.

**Step 3 — Update Form1.cs.** Replace the `ArtificialHorizon` with `AxCombined`:

```csharp
// At top of file, add:
using AxCombinedLib;

// Replace:
private ArtificialHorizon _ahPanel;
// With:
private AxCombined _combined;
```

In `BuildUI()`, replace the ArtificialHorizon block:
```csharp
// Remove:
_ahPanel          = new ArtificialHorizon();
_ahPanel.Location = new Point(10, 10);
_ahPanel.Size     = new Size(220, 220);
this.Controls.Add(_ahPanel);

// Replace with:
_combined          = new AxCombined();
_combined.Location = new Point(10, 10);
_combined.Size     = new Size(480, 436);   // same size as in TESTx
this.Controls.Add(_combined);
```

In `UpdateDisplay()`, replace the AH lines:
```csharp
// Remove:
_ahPanel.Roll  = t1.Roll7Angle;
_ahPanel.Pitch = t1.Pitch7Angle;

// Replace with:
_combined.Roll         = (int)t1.Roll7Angle;
_combined.Pitch        = t1.Pitch7Angle;
_combined.Airspeed     = t1.CAS;
_combined.Altitude     = t1.Hp;
_combined.Heading      = t1.Heading;
// VerticalSpeed from LR Frame 3, packet #3:
byte[] p3 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[2];
if (p3 != null)
{
    TelemetryData t3 = TelemetryDecoder.Decode(p3);
    _combined.VerticalSpeed = t3.ROC_Estimated;
}
_combined.Refresh();
```

**Step 4 — Adjust form width** since the Combined panel is 480px wide (vs 220 for the custom AH). In `BuildUI()`, shift the Flight and GPS groups right:

```csharp
// Change Flight group X from 240 to 500:
GroupBox grpFlight = MakeGroup("FLIGHT INSTRUMENTS",
    new Point(500, 10), new Size(240, 225), Color.Lime);

// Change GPS group X from 490 to 750:
GroupBox grpGPS = MakeGroup("GPS / NAVIGATION",
    new Point(750, 10), new Size(255, 225), Color.Cyan);

// Increase form width:
this.ClientSize = new Size(1200, 490);
```

Also in `ArtificialHorizon.cs` — you can keep the file in the project (no harm), or remove it since it's no longer used.

```

```

[141] CLAUDE
----------------------------------------
Still the same error — likely a **platform mismatch**. ActiveX controls (OCX) are 32-bit, but your project probably targets **AnyCPU** which runs as 64-bit on modern Windows.

Fix — change to x86:

1. In VS, go to **Build** menu → **Configuration Manager**
2. Under **Active solution platform**, click the dropdown → **New...**
3. Select **x86** → OK
4. Close Configuration Manager
5. **Rebuild** and run

**Or** faster way:
1. Right-click project → **Properties**
2. **Build** tab
3. Change **Platform target** from `Any CPU` to `x86`
4. Save → Rebuild → Run

This forces the app to run as 32-bit so it can load the 32-bit ActiveX OCX.

[149] CLAUDE

Yes, exactly — everything is built **programmatically in code** (`BuildUI()`), not through the Visual Studio Designer. That's why you don't see drag-and-drop controls in the Design view.

**Pros of this approach:**
- No `.Designer.cs` file conflicts
- Easy to adjust sizes and positions by changing numbers in code
- Portable — just one `Form1.cs` file

**Cons:**
- Can't drag controls visually in VS Designer
- Have to compile to see layout changes

**If you prefer visual design**, we can migrate — but it requires:
1. Splitting into `Form1.cs` + `Form1.Designer.cs`
2. Moving all control declarations and `BuildUI()` into the Designer format

For a GCS application the programmatic approach is actually common and practical — positions come from ICD/screen layout specs rather than drag-and-drop anyway.

For now, if you want to adjust anything — position, size, colours — just tell me what to move and I'll update the numbers. What would you like to change or do next?

This session is being continued from a previous conversation that ran out of context. The summary below covers the earlier portion of the conversation.

Summary:
1. Primary Request and Intent:
   - (Continued from prior session) Build GCS_240626 WinForms app (.NET Framework 4.8) with event-driven serial reception, CRC-32 validated 164-byte packets, full telemetry decoder from ICD
   - Implement GCS display: flight instruments, GPS/nav, engine/power, link health, artificial horizon
   - Integrate Combined.dll ActiveX PFD control (AxCombinedLib.AxCombined) replacing custom ArtificialHorizon
   - Add Demo Mode with sliders to drive PFD without live data
   - **Most recent request**: Reconfigure layout per Screen layout.txt:
     - Screen 1900 x 1000
     - Font 14 Bold, Neon Green text, Black background
     - Engine & Power on RIGHT side, vertical with 1.5 line spacing
     - Link Health under Engine, same style
     - Flight Instrument Block with specific groupings and field layout (see section 8)

2. Key Technical Concepts:
   - System.IO.Ports.SerialPort event-driven reception (DataReceived)
   - Ring buffer + state machine packet framing (AA 55 DD XX sync header)
   - CRC-32 (seed 0x00000000, reflected poly 0xEDB88320), computed over bytes [0-159], stored little-endian at [160-163]
   - 8 fixed-length 164-byte telemetry packets; stored in `public static readonly byte[][] PacketData = new byte[8][]`
   - TelemetryDecoder: Full Rate [4-61], Half Rate Frame1 (odd pkts) / Frame2 (even pkts) [62-89], Low Rate one-of-8 [90-120]
   - Scaling: `raw / maxRaw * (maxEng - minEng) + minEng`, little-endian unsigned integers
   - AxCombinedLib.AxCombined — ActiveX OCX PFD control; properties: Airspeed, Altitude, Heading, Pitch, Roll, Position (all int); size 384x372
   - Interop via AxInterop.CombinedLib.1.0.dll + Interop.CombinedLib.1.0.dll
   - COM/ActiveX requires 32-bit process (x86 platform target)
   - Programmatic WinForms layout (no Designer); BuildUI() pattern
   - Demo mode flag (`_demoMode`) gates TrackBar inputs vs live telemetry
   - .NET Framework 4.8, C# 7.3 (no nullable reference types, no `?` annotations)

3. Files and Code Sections:

   - **PacketReceiver.cs** (in GCS_240626 project)
     - Existing file from prior session; requires TWO additions:
     ```csharp
     // In class body (with other static fields):
     public static int CRCFailCount = 0;
     
     // In HandlePacket() else-branch (CRC fail path):
     CRCFailCount++;
     ```
     - HandlePacket structure:
     ```csharp
     private void HandlePacket(byte[] packet)
     {
         int packetNum = packet[3];
         if (packetNum < 1 || packetNum > 8) return;
         if (ValidateCRC(packet))
         {
             Array.Copy(packet, PacketData[packetNum - 1], PACKET_LEN);
         }
         else
         {
             CRCFailCount++;
         }
     }
     ```

   - **ArtificialHorizon.cs** (outputs folder, namespace GCS_240626)
     - GDI+ custom Control; double-buffered
     - Properties: `double Roll`, `double Pitch` (both call Invalidate())
     - OnPaint: clip to circle, rotate+translate for roll/pitch, draw sky(RGB 15,100,185)/ground(RGB 110,65,20), horizon line, pitch ladder ±30° every 5°, fixed yellow aircraft symbol, roll arc ±60°, roll pointer triangle
     - No longer used (replaced by AxCombined) but can remain in project

   - **Form1.cs** (most recent version — with Demo Mode)
     ```csharp
     using System;
     using System.Drawing;
     using System.Windows.Forms;
     using AxCombinedLib;
     
     namespace GCS_240626
     {
         public partial class Form1 : Form
         {
             private PacketReceiver _receiver;
             private System.Windows.Forms.Timer _displayTimer;
             private AxCombined _combined;
             private bool _demoMode = false;
     
             // Demo controls
             private Button    _btnDemo;
             private TrackBar  _tbAirspeed, _tbAltitude, _tbHeading;
             private TrackBar  _tbPitch,    _tbRoll,     _tbPosition;
             private Label     _lblDemoAS,  _lblDemoAlt, _lblDemoHdg;
             private Label     _lblDemoPitch, _lblDemoRoll, _lblDemoPos;
     
             // Telemetry labels (Flight, GPS, Engine, Link)
             // ... [all label fields] ...
     
             public Form1()
             {
                 InitializeComponent();
                 this.Load += Form1_Load;
                 this.FormClosing += Form1_FormClosing;
                 BuildUI();
             }
     
             private void Form1_Load(object sender, EventArgs e)
             {
                 _receiver = new PacketReceiver();
                 _receiver.Open("COM1", 115200);
                 _displayTimer = new System.Windows.Forms.Timer();
                 _displayTimer.Interval = 100;
                 _displayTimer.Tick += UpdateDisplay;
                 _displayTimer.Start();
             }
     
             private void BtnDemo_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
             {
                 _demoMode = !_demoMode;
                 if (_demoMode) { _btnDemo.Text = "DEMO: ON"; _btnDemo.BackColor = Color.FromArgb(0,180,0); }
                 else           { _btnDemo.Text = "DEMO: OFF"; _btnDemo.BackColor = Color.FromArgb(60,60,60); }
             }
     
             private void UpdateDisplay(object sender, EventArgs e)
             {
                 if (_demoMode)
                 {
                     _combined.Airspeed = _tbAirspeed.Value;
                     _combined.Altitude = _tbAltitude.Value;
                     _combined.Heading  = _tbHeading.Value;
                     _combined.Pitch    = _tbPitch.Value;
                     _combined.Roll     = _tbRoll.Value;
                     _combined.Refresh();
                     // update numeric labels from slider values
                     return;
                 }
                 // LIVE mode: decode packets, set Combined + labels
                 byte[] p1 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[0];
                 if (p1 == null) return;
                 TelemetryData t1 = TelemetryDecoder.Decode(p1);
                 _combined.Roll     = (int)t1.Roll7Angle;
                 _combined.Pitch    = (int)t1.Pitch7Angle;
                 _combined.Airspeed = (int)t1.CAS;
                 _combined.Altitude = (int)t1.Hp;
                 _combined.Heading  = (int)t1.Heading;
                 _combined.Refresh();
                 // ... update all labels from t1, t2(p2), t6(p6), t7(p7), t8(p8) ...
             }
     
             private void BuildUI()
             {
                 this.ClientSize = new Size(1250, 640);
                 this.BackColor  = Color.FromArgb(25, 25, 25);
                 // AxCombined at (10,10) size 384x372
                 // Flight group at (404,10) size 235x225
                 // GPS group at (649,10) size 325x225
                 // Demo panel at (984,10) size 255x500
                 // Engine group at (10,390) size 960x120
                 // Link group at (10,520) size 960x100
             }
     
             private void BuildDemoPanel()
             {
                 // GroupBox at (984,10) 255x500, magenta border
                 // _btnDemo toggle button
                 // 6 TrackBars via AddSlider():
                 //   Airspeed  0-100,  Altitude -1000-11000,  Heading 0-360
                 //   Pitch -30-30,     Roll -60-60,           Position 0-100
             }
         }
     }
     ```

[167] USER
----------------------------------------
Which variable is responsible for maintaining gaps between rows? I want to reduce the gap

[168] CLAUDE
----------------------------------------
Two constants at the top of `BuildFlightBlock()` control row spacing:

```csharp
private const int FL_ROW  = 30;   // gap between rows in Attitude / Height / Speed sections
private const int GPS_ROW = 22;   // gap between rows in the GPS section (already compressed)
```

`FL_ROW = 30` is the one affecting most of the display. Reduce it — e.g. to **24 or 26** — and all the Attitude, Height, and Speed rows will tighten up. `GPS_ROW = 22` is already smaller; you can reduce that too if needed.

The label height `FL_H = 24` should stay ≤ `FL_ROW`, otherwise labels will overlap. A safe pairing:

| FL_ROW | FL_H | Effect |
|--------|------|--------|
| 30 | 24 | current (6 px gap) |
| 26 | 22 | tighter |
| 24 | 20 | very tight |

using System;
using System.Drawing;
using System.Windows.Forms;
using AxCombinedLib;
// ============================================================
//  Form1.cs  –  GCS_240626
//  Screen  : 1900 x 1000
//  Font    : Consolas 14pt Bold, Neon Green on Black
//
//  Layout
//  ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
//   x=10   PFD (384×372)           │  MAP (1010×452)    │  ENGINE (455×295)
//   x=10   [DEMO btn] (384×40)     │                    │  LINK   (455×230)
//   x=10   [DEMO sliders — hidden] │                    │
//   ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
//          FLIGHT BLOCK (1010×522)  bottom-centre
//
//  Demo behaviour
//  ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
//  • "DEMO ▶ OFF" button is ALWAYS visible below the PFD.
//  • Click once  → slider panel appears, demo mode ON.
//  • Click again → slider panel hides, live mode resumes.
// ============================================================
namespace GCS_240626
{
    public partial class Form1 : Form
    {
        // ── Serial & timer ───────────────────────────────────────────────
        private PacketReceiver _receiver;
        private System.Windows.Forms.Timer _displayTimer;
        // ── Controls ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

        private MapControl _mapCtrl;
        // ── Demo ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

        private Button _btnDemo;          // always visible
        private Panel _pnlSliders;       // hidden until DEMO ON
        private TrackBar _tbAirspeed, _tbAltitude, _tbHeading, _tbPitch, _tbRoll, _tbPosition;
        private Label _lblDemoAS, _lblDemoAlt, _lblDemoHdg, _lblDemoPitch, _lblDemoRoll, _lblDemoPos;
        // ── Flight block value labels ─────────────────────────────────────
        private Label _valLat, _valLon, _valD2Base, _valOffTrack, _valGPS, _valWP;
        private Label _valRollAngle, _valRollCmd, _valPitchAngle, _valPitchCmd;
        private Label _valHeading, _valHeadingCmd;
        private Label _valAileron, _valFlap;
        private Label _valHMSL, _valHCmd, _valHAGL, _valRA;
        private Label _valElevator, _valROC;
        private Label _valSpeed, _valSpeedCmd, _valThrottle;
        // ── Engine & Power value labels ──────────────────────────────────

        private Label _valBattV, _valAltV, _valCHTL, _valCHTR;
        // ── Link Health value labels ─────────────────────────────────────

        private static readonly Font FNT11 = new Font("Consolas", 11f, FontStyle.Bold);
        private static readonly Font FNT10 = new Font("Consolas", 10f);

        private static readonly Color WHITE = Color.White;
        private static readonly Color CYAN = Color.Cyan;
        private static readonly Color BLACK = Color.Black;

        private void Form1_Load(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            _receiver = new PacketReceiver();
            _receiver.Open("COM11", 115200);
            _displayTimer = new System.Windows.Forms.Timer();
            _displayTimer.Interval = 100;
            _displayTimer.Tick += UpdateDisplay;
            _displayTimer.Start();
        }
        private void Form1_FormClosing(object sender, FormClosingEventArgs e)
        {
            if (_displayTimer != null) _displayTimer.Stop();
            if (_receiver != null) _receiver.Close();
        }
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  Demo toggle
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        private void BtnDemo_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            _demoMode = !_demoMode;
            if (_demoMode)
            {
                _btnDemo.Text = "DEMO  ■  ON   (click to hide sliders)";
                _btnDemo.BackColor = Color.FromArgb(0, 150, 0);
                _btnDemo.ForeColor = WHITE;
            }
            else
            {
                _btnDemo.Text = "DEMO  ▶  OFF  (click to show sliders)";
                _btnDemo.BackColor = Color.FromArgb(40, 40, 40);
                _btnDemo.ForeColor = LIME;
            }
            _pnlSliders.Visible = _demoMode;   // show/hide slider section
        }
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  Display update  (100 ms timer)
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        private void UpdateDisplay(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            if (_demoMode)
            {
                _combined.Airspeed = _tbAirspeed.Value;
                _combined.Altitude = _tbAltitude.Value;
                _combined.Heading = _tbHeading.Value;
                _combined.Pitch = _tbPitch.Value;
                _combined.Roll = _tbRoll.Value;
                _combined.Refresh();
                _valRollAngle.Text = _tbRoll.Value + "°";
                _valPitchAngle.Text = _tbPitch.Value + "°";
                _valHeading.Text = _tbHeading.Value + "°";
                _valHMSL.Text = _tbAltitude.Value + " m";
                _valSpeed.Text = _tbAirspeed.Value + " m/s";
                return;
            }
            // ── Live telemetry ───────────────────────────────────────────
            byte[] p1 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[0];
            byte[] p2 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[1];
            byte[] p3 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[2];
            byte[] p5 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[4];
            byte[] p6 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[5];
            byte[] p7 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[6];
            byte[] p8 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[7];
            if (p1 == null) return;
            TelemetryData t1 = TelemetryDecoder.Decode(p1);
            _combined.Roll = (int)t1.Roll7Angle;
            _combined.Pitch = (int)t1.Pitch7Angle;
            _combined.Airspeed = (int)t1.CAS;
            _combined.Altitude = (int)t1.Hp;
            _combined.Heading = (int)t1.Heading;
            _combined.Refresh();
            _mapCtrl.UpdatePosition(t1.Latitude, t1.Longitude, t1.Heading);
            _valLat.Text = t1.Latitude.ToString("F4") + "°";
            _valLon.Text = t1.Longitude.ToString("F4") + "°";
            _valRollAngle.Text = t1.Roll7Angle.ToString("F1") + "°";
            _valRollCmd.Text = t1.Phi_Com.ToString("F1") + "°";
            _valPitchAngle.Text = t1.Pitch7Angle.ToString("F1") + "°";
            _valPitchCmd.Text = t1.Theta_Cmd.ToString("F1") + "°";
            _valHeading.Text = t1.Heading.ToString("F0") + "°";
            _valHeadingCmd.Text = t1.Psi_Com.ToString("F0") + "°";
            _valAileron.Text = t1.Inner_SB_Ail_Com.ToString("F1");
            _valFlap.Text = "N/A";
            _valHMSL.Text = t1.Hp.ToString("F0") + " m";
            _valHCmd.Text = t1.Alt_Com.ToString("F0") + " m";
            _valHAGL.Text = t1.AGL.ToString("F1") + " m";
            _valRA.Text = t1.Radar_Alt.ToString("F1") + " m";
            _valElevator.Text = t1.Top_SB_RV_Com.ToString("F1");
            _valSpeed.Text = t1.CAS.ToString("F1") + " m/s";
            _valSpeedCmd.Text = t1.CAS_Com.ToString("F1") + " m/s";
            _valThrottle.Text = (t1.Throttle_pos * 100.0).ToString("F0") + " %";
            _valRPM.Text = t1.Engine_RPM.ToString("F0") + " rpm";
            _valBattV.Text = t1.Batt_Volts.ToString("F1") + " V";
            _valAltV.Text = t1.Alt_Volts.ToString("F1") + " V";
            if (p2 != null)
            {
                TelemetryData t2 = TelemetryDecoder.Decode(p2);
                _valD2Base.Text = t2.Distance7From7Base.ToString("F1") + " km";
                _valOffTrack.Text = t2.OffTrack.ToString("F1") + " m";
                _valWP.Text = t2.D2Go.ToString("F1") + " km";
            }
            if (p3 != null)
            {
                TelemetryData t3 = TelemetryDecoder.Decode(p3);
                _valROC.Text = t3.ROC_Estimated.ToString("F1") + " m/s";
            }
            if (p5 != null)
            {
                TelemetryData t5 = TelemetryDecoder.Decode(p5);
                _valGPS.Text = t5.Solution7Status > 0 ? "DIFF" : "SINGLE";
            }
            if (p6 != null)
            {
                TelemetryData t6 = TelemetryDecoder.Decode(p6);
                _valFuelMain.Text = (t6.FuelLevel_Main * 100).ToString("F0") + " %";
                _valFuelLeft.Text = (t6.FuelLevel_Left * 100).ToString("F0") + " %";
                _valFuelRight.Text = (t6.FuelLevel_Right * 100).ToString("F0") + " %";
                _valCHTL.Text = t6.CHT7Left.ToString("F0") + " °C";
                _valCHTR.Text = t6.CHT7Right.ToString("F0") + " °C";
            }
            _valCRCFail.Text = PacketReceiver.CRCFailCount.ToString();
            _valPktNum.Text = t1.PacketNumber.ToString();
            if (p7 != null)
            {
                TelemetryData t7 = TelemetryDecoder.Decode(p7);
                _valGPSMiss.Text = t7.GPSMissPacketsCount.ToString();
                _valVGMiss.Text = t7.VGMissPacketsCount.ToString();
            }
            if (p8 != null)
            {
                TelemetryData t8 = TelemetryDecoder.Decode(p8);
                _valGPSRate.Text = t8.GPSPacketRate.ToString("F0") + " pkt/s";
                _valVGRate.Text = t8.VGPacketRate.ToString("F0") + " pkt/s";
            }
        }

            _valHAGL = FL(pnl, "----", FL_VX, y, FL_VW, FL_H, WHITE);
            FLn(pnl, "ROC:", FL_R_NX, y, FL_R_NW, FL_H, LIME, ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft);
            _valROC = FL(pnl, "----", FL_R_VX, y, FL_R_VW, FL_H, WHITE);
            FL(pnl, "[m/s]", FL_UX, y, 80, FL_H, CYAN);
            y += FL_ROW;
            FLn(pnl, "RA:", FL_NX, y, FL_NW, FL_H, LIME, ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft);
            _valRA = FL(pnl, "----", FL_VX, y, FL_VW, FL_H, WHITE);
            y += FL_ROW + 4; Sep(pnl, 5, y, 998);
            // ── SPEED ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
            y += 7;
            FLn(pnl, "Speed:", FL_NX, y, FL_NW, FL_H, LIME, ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft);
            _valSpeed = FL(pnl, "----", FL_VX, y, FL_VW, FL_H, WHITE);
            FL(pnl, "Sensor in Use:", FL_R_NX, y, 130, FL_H, CYAN);
            FL(pnl, "[ADS]", FL_R_NX + 133, y, 100, FL_H, WHITE);
            y += FL_ROW;
            FLn(pnl, "Speed CMD:", FL_NX, y, FL_NW, FL_H, LIME, ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft);
            _valSpeedCmd = FL(pnl, "----", FL_VX, y, FL_VW, FL_H, WHITE);
            y += FL_ROW;
            FLn(pnl, "Throttle:", FL_NX, y, FL_NW, FL_H, LIME, ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft);
            _valThrottle = FL(pnl, "----", FL_VX, y, FL_VW, FL_H, WHITE);
        }
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  Right column: Engine & Power + Link Health
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        private void BuildRightPanel()
        {
            const int ROW = 30, H = 24, NX = 8, NW = 130, VX = 142, VW = 300;
            var grpEng = MakeGroupBox("ENGINE & POWER", 1430, 10, 455, 295, Color.Orange, FNT14);
            int y = 34;
            EngRow(grpEng, "RPM:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valRPM); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpEng, "Fuel Main:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valFuelMain); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpEng, "Fuel Left:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valFuelLeft); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpEng, "Fuel Right:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valFuelRight); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpEng, "Batt V:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valBattV); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpEng, "Alt V:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valAltV); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpEng, "CHT Left:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valCHTL); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpEng, "CHT Right:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valCHTR);
            this.Controls.Add(grpEng);
            var grpLink = MakeGroupBox("LINK HEALTH", 1430, 315, 455, 230, Color.Yellow, FNT14);
            y = 34;
            EngRow(grpLink, "CRC Fails:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valCRCFail); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpLink, "GPS Miss:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valGPSMiss); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpLink, "VG Miss:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valVGMiss); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpLink, "GPS Rate:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valGPSRate); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpLink, "VG Rate:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valVGRate); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpLink, "Last Pkt #:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valPktNum);
            this.Controls.Add(grpLink);
        }
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  Helpers
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        private Label FL(Control p, string t, int x, int y, int w, int h, Color fg)
        {
            var l = new Label
            {
                Text = t,
                Location = new Point(x, y),
                Size = new Size(w, h),
                ForeColor = fg,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT14
            };
            p.Controls.Add(l); return l;
        }
        private Label FLn(Control p, string t, int x, int y, int w, int h,
                           Color fg, ContentAlignment a)
        {
            var l = new Label
            {
                Text = t,
                Location = new Point(x, y),
                Size = new Size(w, h),
                ForeColor = fg,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT14,
                TextAlign = a
            };
            p.Controls.Add(l); return l;
        }
        private Label FLg(Control p, string t, int x, int y, int w, int h,
                           Color fg, ContentAlignment a)
        {
            var l = new Label
            {
                Text = t,
                Location = new Point(x, y),
                Size = new Size(w, h),
                ForeColor = fg,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT12,
                TextAlign = a
            };
            p.Controls.Add(l); return l;
        }
        private void Sep(Control p, int x, int y, int w)
        {
            p.Controls.Add(new Panel
            {
                Location = new Point(x, y),
                Size = new Size(w, 2),
                BackColor = Color.FromArgb(0, 140, 0)
            });
        }
        private void EngRow(Control parent, string name, int nx, int y, int nw, int h,
                             int vx, int vw, out Label valLabel)
        {
            parent.Controls.Add(new Label
            {
                Text = name,
                Location = new Point(nx, y),
                Size = new Size(nw, h),
                ForeColor = LIME,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT14,
                TextAlign = ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft
            });
            var val = new Label
            {
                Text = "----",
                Location = new Point(vx, y),
                Size = new Size(vw, h),
                ForeColor = WHITE,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT14
            };
            parent.Controls.Add(val);
            valLabel = val;
        }
        private GroupBox MakeGroupBox(string title, int x, int y, int w, int h,
                                       Color tc, Font f)
        {
            return new GroupBox
            {
                Text = title,
                Location = new Point(x, y),
                Size = new Size(w, h),
                ForeColor = tc,
                BackColor = Color.FromArgb(12, 12, 12),
                Font = f
            };
        }
        private TrackBar DemoSlider(Control parent, string name, int min, int max,
                                     int sv, int y, out Label valueLabel)
        {
            parent.Controls.Add(new Label
            {
                Text = name,
                Location = new Point(6, y),
                Size = new Size(220, 20),
                ForeColor = Color.Silver,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT10
            });
            var vl = new Label
            {
                Text = sv.ToString(),
                Location = new Point(228, y),
                Size = new Size(148, 20),
                ForeColor = WHITE,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT11,
                TextAlign = ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft
            };
            parent.Controls.Add(vl);
            var tb = new TrackBar
            {
                Minimum = min,
                Maximum = max,
                Value = sv,
                TickFrequency = Math.Max(1, (max - min) / 10),
                SmallChange = 1,
                LargeChange = Math.Max(1, (max - min) / 20),
                Location = new Point(4, y + 22),
                Size = new Size(372, 36),
                BackColor = Color.FromArgb(30, 30, 30)
            };
            Label cap = vl;
            tb.ValueChanged += (s, ev) => cap.Text = ((TrackBar)s).Value.ToString();
            parent.Controls.Add(tb);
            valueLabel = vl;
            return tb;
        }
    }
}

attaching the modified code of form1.cs.... using System;
using System.Drawing;
using System.Windows.Forms;
using AxCombinedLib;
// ============================================================
//  Form1.cs  –  GCS_240626
//  Screen  : 1900 x 1000
//  Font    : Consolas 14pt Bold, Neon Green on Black
//
//  Layout
//  ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

namespace GCS_240626
{
    public partial class Form1 : Form
    {
        // ── Serial & timer ───────────────────────────────────────────────

        private static readonly Font FNT12 = new Font("Consolas", 12f, FontStyle.Bold);
        private static readonly Font FNT11 = new Font("Consolas", 11f, FontStyle.Bold);
        private static readonly Font FNT10 = new Font("Consolas", 10f);
        private static readonly Color LIME = Color.Lime;
        private static readonly Color WHITE = Color.White;
        private static readonly Color CYAN = Color.Cyan;
        private static readonly Color BLACK = Color.Black;
        // ── Flight Block column constants ─────────────────────────────────
        private const int FL_NX = 5;
        private const int FL_NW = 137;// Uzair215;
        private const int FL_VX = 145;// uzair 223;

        private const int FL_R_VX = 350; //300; // Uzair 350;  // Uzair 663;

        public Form1()

            this.Load += Form1_Load;
            this.FormClosing += Form1_FormClosing;
            BuildUI();
        }
        private void Form1_Load(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            _receiver = new PacketReceiver();
            _receiver.Open("COM11", 115200);
            _displayTimer = new System.Windows.Forms.Timer();
            _displayTimer.Interval = 100;
            _displayTimer.Tick += UpdateDisplay;
            _displayTimer.Start();
        }
        private void Form1_FormClosing(object sender, FormClosingEventArgs e)
        {
            if (_displayTimer != null) _displayTimer.Stop();
            if (_receiver != null) _receiver.Close();
        }
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  Demo toggle
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        private void BtnDemo_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            _demoMode = !_demoMode;
            if (_demoMode)
            {
                _btnDemo.Text = "DEMO  ■  ON   (click to hide sliders)";
                _btnDemo.BackColor = Color.FromArgb(0, 150, 0);
                _btnDemo.ForeColor = WHITE;
            }
            else
            {
                _btnDemo.Text = "DEMO  ▶  OFF  (click to show sliders)";
                _btnDemo.BackColor = Color.FromArgb(40, 40, 40);
                _btnDemo.ForeColor = LIME;
            }
            _pnlSliders.Visible = _demoMode;   // show/hide slider section
        }
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  Display update  (100 ms timer)
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        private void UpdateDisplay(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            if (_demoMode)
            {
                _combined.Airspeed = _tbAirspeed.Value;
                _combined.Altitude = _tbAltitude.Value;
                _combined.Heading = _tbHeading.Value;
                _combined.Pitch = _tbPitch.Value;
                _combined.Roll = _tbRoll.Value;
                _combined.Refresh();
                _valRollAngle.Text = _tbRoll.Value + "°";
                _valPitchAngle.Text = _tbPitch.Value + "°";
                _valHeading.Text = _tbHeading.Value + "°";
                _valHMSL.Text = _tbAltitude.Value + " m";
                _valSpeed.Text = _tbAirspeed.Value + " m/s";
                return;
            }
            // ── Live telemetry ───────────────────────────────────────────
            byte[] p1 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[0];
            byte[] p2 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[1];
            byte[] p3 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[2];
            byte[] p5 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[4];
            byte[] p6 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[5];
            byte[] p7 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[6];
            byte[] p8 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[7];
            if (p1 == null) return;
            TelemetryData t1 = TelemetryDecoder.Decode(p1);
            _combined.Roll = (int)t1.Roll7Angle;
            _combined.Pitch = (int)t1.Pitch7Angle;
            _combined.Airspeed = (int)t1.CAS;
            _combined.Altitude = (int)t1.Hp;
            _combined.Heading = (int)t1.Heading;
            _combined.Refresh();
            _mapCtrl.UpdatePosition(t1.Latitude, t1.Longitude, t1.Heading);
            _valLat.Text = t1.Latitude.ToString("F4") + "°";
            _valLon.Text = t1.Longitude.ToString("F4") + "°";
            _valRollAngle.Text = t1.Roll7Angle.ToString("F1") + "°";
            _valRollCmd.Text = t1.Phi_Com.ToString("F1") + "°";
            _valPitchAngle.Text = t1.Pitch7Angle.ToString("F1") + "°";
            _valPitchCmd.Text = t1.Theta_Cmd.ToString("F1") + "°";
            _valHeading.Text = t1.Heading.ToString("F0") + "°";
            _valHeadingCmd.Text = t1.Psi_Com.ToString("F0") + "°";
            _valAileron.Text = t1.Inner_SB_Ail_Com.ToString("F1");
            _valFlap.Text = "N/A";
            _valHMSL.Text = t1.Hp.ToString("F0") + " m";
            _valHCmd.Text = t1.Alt_Com.ToString("F0") + " m";
            _valHAGL.Text = t1.AGL.ToString("F1") + " m";
            _valRA.Text = t1.Radar_Alt.ToString("F1") + " m";
            _valElevator.Text = t1.Top_SB_RV_Com.ToString("F1");
            _valSpeed.Text = t1.CAS.ToString("F1") + " m/s";
            _valSpeedCmd.Text = t1.CAS_Com.ToString("F1") + " m/s";
            _valThrottle.Text = (t1.Throttle_pos * 100.0).ToString("F0") + " %";
            _valRPM.Text = t1.Engine_RPM.ToString("F0") + " rpm";
            _valBattV.Text = t1.Batt_Volts.ToString("F1") + " V";
            _valAltV.Text = t1.Alt_Volts.ToString("F1") + " V";
            if (p2 != null)
            {
                TelemetryData t2 = TelemetryDecoder.Decode(p2);
                _valD2Base.Text = t2.Distance7From7Base.ToString("F1") + " km";
                _valOffTrack.Text = t2.OffTrack.ToString("F1") + " m";
                _valWP.Text = t2.D2Go.ToString("F1") + " km";
            }
            if (p3 != null)
            {
                TelemetryData t3 = TelemetryDecoder.Decode(p3);
                _valROC.Text = t3.ROC_Estimated.ToString("F1") + " m/s";
            }
            if (p5 != null)
            {
                TelemetryData t5 = TelemetryDecoder.Decode(p5);
                _valGPS.Text = t5.Solution7Status > 0 ? "DIFF" : "SINGLE";
            }
            if (p6 != null)
            {
                TelemetryData t6 = TelemetryDecoder.Decode(p6);
                _valFuelMain.Text = (t6.FuelLevel_Main * 100).ToString("F0") + " %";
                _valFuelLeft.Text = (t6.FuelLevel_Left * 100).ToString("F0") + " %";
                _valFuelRight.Text = (t6.FuelLevel_Right * 100).ToString("F0") + " %";
                _valCHTL.Text = t6.CHT7Left.ToString("F0") + " °C";
                _valCHTR.Text = t6.CHT7Right.ToString("F0") + " °C";
            }
            _valCRCFail.Text = PacketReceiver.CRCFailCount.ToString();
            _valPktNum.Text = t1.PacketNumber.ToString();
            if (p7 != null)
            {
                TelemetryData t7 = TelemetryDecoder.Decode(p7);
                _valGPSMiss.Text = t7.GPSMissPacketsCount.ToString();
                _valVGMiss.Text = t7.VGMissPacketsCount.ToString();
            }
            if (p8 != null)
            {
                TelemetryData t8 = TelemetryDecoder.Decode(p8);
                _valGPSRate.Text = t8.GPSPacketRate.ToString("F0") + " pkt/s";
                _valVGRate.Text = t8.VGPacketRate.ToString("F0") + " pkt/s";
            }
        }
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  BuildUI
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        private void BuildUI()
        {
            this.Text = "GCS_240626 — Ground Control Station";
            this.ClientSize = new Size(1900, 1000);
            this.MinimumSize = new Size(1900, 1040);
            this.BackColor = BLACK;
            this.ForeColor = LIME;
            this.Font = FNT14;
            // PFD  (top-left)
            _combined = new AxCombined();
            _combined.Location = new Point(10, 10);
            _combined.Size = new Size(384, 372);
            ((System.ComponentModel.ISupportInitialize)_combined).BeginInit();
            this.Controls.Add(_combined);
            ((System.ComponentModel.ISupportInitialize)_combined).EndInit();
            BuildDemoButton();    // always-visible toggle below PFD
            BuildDemoSliders();   // slider panel — Visible=false by default
            BuildMapPanel();
            BuildFlightBlock();
            BuildRightPanel();
        }
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

        }
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

        private void BuildRightPanel()

            EngRow(grpLink, "Last Pkt #:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valPktNum);
            this.Controls.Add(grpLink);
        }
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  Helpers
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        private Label FL(Control p, string t, int x, int y, int w, int h, Color fg)
        {
            var l = new Label
            {
                Text = t,
                Location = new Point(x, y),
                Size = new Size(w, h),
                ForeColor = fg,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT14
            };
            p.Controls.Add(l); return l;
        }
        private Label FLn(Control p, string t, int x, int y, int w, int h,
                           Color fg, ContentAlignment a)
        {
            var l = new Label
            {
                Text = t,
                Location = new Point(x, y),
                Size = new Size(w, h),
                ForeColor = fg,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT14,
                TextAlign = a
            };
            p.Controls.Add(l); return l;
        }
        private Label FLg(Control p, string t, int x, int y, int w, int h,
                           Color fg, ContentAlignment a)
        {
            var l = new Label
            {
                Text = t,
                Location = new Point(x, y),
                Size = new Size(w, h),
                ForeColor = fg,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT12,
                TextAlign = a
            };
            p.Controls.Add(l); return l;
        }
        private void Sep(Control p, int x, int y, int w)
        {
            p.Controls.Add(new Panel
            {
                Location = new Point(x, y),
                Size = new Size(w, 2),
                BackColor = Color.FromArgb(0, 140, 0)
            });
        }
        private void EngRow(Control parent, string name, int nx, int y, int nw, int h,
                             int vx, int vw, out Label valLabel)
        {
            parent.Controls.Add(new Label
            {
                Text = name,
                Location = new Point(nx, y),
                Size = new Size(nw, h),
                ForeColor = LIME,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT14,
                TextAlign = ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft
            });
            var val = new Label
            {
                Text = "----",
                Location = new Point(vx, y),
                Size = new Size(vw, h),
                ForeColor = WHITE,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT14
            };
            parent.Controls.Add(val);
            valLabel = val;
        }
        private GroupBox MakeGroupBox(string title, int x, int y, int w, int h,
                                       Color tc, Font f)
        {
            return new GroupBox
            {
                Text = title,
                Location = new Point(x, y),
                Size = new Size(w, h),
                ForeColor = tc,
                BackColor = Color.FromArgb(12, 12, 12),
                Font = f
            };
        }
        private TrackBar DemoSlider(Control parent, string name, int min, int max,
                                     int sv, int y, out Label valueLabel)
        {
            parent.Controls.Add(new Label
            {
                Text = name,
                Location = new Point(6, y),
                Size = new Size(220, 20),
                ForeColor = Color.Silver,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT10
            });
            var vl = new Label
            {
                Text = sv.ToString(),
                Location = new Point(228, y),
                Size = new Size(148, 20),
                ForeColor = WHITE,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT11,
                TextAlign = ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft
            };
            parent.Controls.Add(vl);
            var tb = new TrackBar
            {
                Minimum = min,
                Maximum = max,
                Value = sv,
                TickFrequency = Math.Max(1, (max - min) / 10),
                SmallChange = 1,
                LargeChange = Math.Max(1, (max - min) / 20),
                Location = new Point(4, y + 22),
                Size = new Size(372, 36),
                BackColor = Color.FromArgb(30, 30, 30)
            };
            Label cap = vl;
            tb.ValueChanged += (s, ev) => cap.Text = ((TrackBar)s).Value.ToString();
            parent.Controls.Add(tb);
            valueLabel = vl;
            return tb;
        }
    }
}

using System;
using System.Drawing;
using System.Windows.Forms;
using AxCombinedLib;
// ============================================================
//  Form1.cs  –  GCS_240626
//  Screen  : 1900 x 1000
//  Font    : Consolas 14pt Bold, Neon Green on Black
//
//  Layout
//  ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
//   x=10   PFD (384×372)           │  MAP (1010×452)    │  ENGINE (455×295)
//   x=10   [DEMO btn] (384×40)     │                    │  LINK   (455×230)
//   x=10   [DEMO sliders — hidden] │                    │
//   ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
//          FLIGHT BLOCK (1010×522)  bottom-centre
//
//  Demo behaviour
//  ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
//  • "DEMO ▶ OFF" button is ALWAYS visible below the PFD.
//  • Click once  → slider panel appears, demo mode ON.
//  • Click again → slider panel hides, live mode resumes.
// ============================================================
namespace GCS_240626
{
    public partial class Form1 : Form
    {
        // ── Serial & timer ───────────────────────────────────────────────
        private PacketReceiver _receiver;
        private System.Windows.Forms.Timer _displayTimer;
        // ── Controls ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
        private AxCombined _combined;
        private MapControl _mapCtrl;
        // ── Demo ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
        private bool _demoMode = false;
        private Button _btnDemo;          // always visible
        private Panel _pnlSliders;       // hidden until DEMO ON
        private TrackBar _tbAirspeed, _tbAltitude, _tbHeading, _tbPitch, _tbRoll, _tbPosition;
        private Label _lblDemoAS, _lblDemoAlt, _lblDemoHdg, _lblDemoPitch, _lblDemoRoll, _lblDemoPos;
        // ── Flight block value labels ─────────────────────────────────────
        private Label _valLat, _valLon, _valD2Base, _valOffTrack, _valGPS, _valWP;
        private Label _valRollAngle, _valRollCmd, _valPitchAngle, _valPitchCmd;
        private Label _valHeading, _valHeadingCmd;
        private Label _valAileron, _valFlap;
        private Label _valHMSL, _valHCmd, _valHAGL, _valRA;
        private Label _valElevator, _valROC;
        private Label _valSpeed, _valSpeedCmd, _valThrottle;
        // ── Engine & Power value labels ──────────────────────────────────
        private Label _valRPM, _valFuelMain, _valFuelLeft, _valFuelRight;
        private Label _valBattV, _valAltV, _valCHTL, _valCHTR;
        // ── Link Health value labels ─────────────────────────────────────
        private Label _valCRCFail, _valGPSMiss, _valVGMiss;
        private Label _valGPSRate, _valVGRate, _valPktNum;
        // ── Fonts & colours ──────────────────────────────────────────────
        private static readonly Font FNT14 = new Font("Consolas", 14f, FontStyle.Bold);
        private static readonly Font FNT12 = new Font("Consolas", 12f, FontStyle.Bold);
        private static readonly Font FNT11 = new Font("Consolas", 11f, FontStyle.Bold);
        private static readonly Font FNT10 = new Font("Consolas", 10f);
        private static readonly Color LIME = Color.Lime;
        private static readonly Color WHITE = Color.White;
        private static readonly Color CYAN = Color.Cyan;
        private static readonly Color BLACK = Color.Black;
        // ── Flight Block column constants ─────────────────────────────────
        private const int FL_NX = 5;
        private const int FL_NW = 137;
        private const int FL_VX = 145;
        private const int FL_VW = 95;
        private const int FL_R_NX = 250;
        private const int FL_R_NW = 105;
        private const int FL_R_VX = 350;
        private const int FL_R_VW = 130;
        private const int FL_UX = 603;
        private const int FL_H = 24;
        private const int FL_ROW = 27;
        // ── GPS section (12pt, compressed) ──────────────────────────────
        private const int GPS_ROW = 27;
        private const int GPS_H = 24;
        // ── Constructor ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
        public Form1()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
            this.Load += Form1_Load;
            this.FormClosing += Form1_FormClosing;
            BuildUI();
        }
        private void Form1_Load(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            _receiver = new PacketReceiver();
            _receiver.Open("COM11", 115200);
            _displayTimer = new System.Windows.Forms.Timer();
            _displayTimer.Interval = 100;
            _displayTimer.Tick += UpdateDisplay;
            _displayTimer.Start();
        }
        private void Form1_FormClosing(object sender, FormClosingEventArgs e)
        {
            if (_displayTimer != null) _displayTimer.Stop();
            if (_receiver != null) _receiver.Close();
        }
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  Demo toggle
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        private void BtnDemo_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            _demoMode = !_demoMode;
            if (_demoMode)
            {
                _btnDemo.Text = "DEMO  ■  ON   (click to hide sliders)";
                _btnDemo.BackColor = Color.FromArgb(0, 150, 0);
                _btnDemo.ForeColor = WHITE;
            }
            else
            {
                _btnDemo.Text = "DEMO  ▶  OFF  (click to show sliders)";
                _btnDemo.BackColor = Color.FromArgb(40, 40, 40);
                _btnDemo.ForeColor = LIME;
            }
            _pnlSliders.Visible = _demoMode;
        }
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  Display update  (100 ms timer)
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        private void UpdateDisplay(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            if (_demoMode)
            {
                _combined.Airspeed = _tbAirspeed.Value;
                _combined.Altitude = _tbAltitude.Value;
                _combined.Heading = _tbHeading.Value;
                _combined.Pitch = _tbPitch.Value;
                _combined.Roll = _tbRoll.Value;
                _combined.Refresh();
                _valRollAngle.Text = _tbRoll.Value + "°";
                _valPitchAngle.Text = _tbPitch.Value + "°";
                _valHeading.Text = _tbHeading.Value + "°";
                _valHMSL.Text = _tbAltitude.Value + " m";
                _valSpeed.Text = _tbAirspeed.Value + " m/s";
                return;
            }
            // ── Live telemetry ───────────────────────────────────────────
            byte[] p1 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[0];
            byte[] p2 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[1];
            byte[] p3 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[2];
            byte[] p5 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[4];
            byte[] p6 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[5];
            byte[] p7 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[6];
            byte[] p8 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[7];
            if (p1 == null) return;
            TelemetryData t1 = TelemetryDecoder.Decode(p1);
            _combined.Roll = (int)t1.Roll7Angle;
            _combined.Pitch = (int)t1.Pitch7Angle;
            _combined.Airspeed = (int)t1.CAS;
            _combined.Altitude = (int)t1.Hp;
            _combined.Heading = (int)t1.Heading;
            _combined.Refresh();
            _mapCtrl.UpdatePosition(t1.Latitude, t1.Longitude, t1.Heading);
            _valLat.Text = t1.Latitude.ToString("F4") + "°";
            _valLon.Text = t1.Longitude.ToString("F4") + "°";
            _valRollAngle.Text = t1.Roll7Angle.ToString("F1") + "°";
            _valRollCmd.Text = t1.Phi_Com.ToString("F1") + "°";
            _valPitchAngle.Text = t1.Pitch7Angle.ToString("F1") + "°";
            _valPitchCmd.Text = t1.Theta_Cmd.ToString("F1") + "°";
            _valHeading.Text = t1.Heading.ToString("F0") + "°";
