        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  Helpers
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        private Label FL(Control p, string t, int x, int y, int w, int h, Color fg)
        {
            var l = new Label
            {
                Text = t,
                Location = new Point(x, y),
                Size = new Size(w, h),
                ForeColor = fg,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT14
            };
            p.Controls.Add(l);
            return l;
        }
        private Label FLn(Control p, string t, int x, int y, int w, int h,
                           Color fg, ContentAlignment a)
        {
            var l = new Label
            {
                Text = t,
                Location = new Point(x, y),
                Size = new Size(w, h),
                ForeColor = fg,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT14,
                TextAlign = a
            };
            p.Controls.Add(l);
            return l;
        }
        private Label FLg(Control p, string t, int x, int y, int w, int h,
                           Color fg, ContentAlignment a)
        {
            var l = new Label
            {
                Text = t,
                Location = new Point(x, y),
                Size = new Size(w, h),
                ForeColor = fg,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT14,
                TextAlign = a
            };
            p.Controls.Add(l);
            return l;
        }
        private void Sep(Control p, int x, int y, int w)
        {
            p.Controls.Add(new Panel
            {
                Location = new Point(x, y),
                Size = new Size(w, 2),
                BackColor = Color.FromArgb(0, 140, 0)
            });
        }
        private void EngRow(Control parent, string name, int nx, int y, int nw, int h,
                             int vx, int vw, out Label valLabel)
        {
            parent.Controls.Add(new Label
            {
                Text = name,
                Location = new Point(nx, y),
                Size = new Size(nw, h),
                ForeColor = LIME,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT14,
                TextAlign = ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft
            });
            var val = new Label
            {
                Text = "----",
                Location = new Point(vx, y),
                Size = new Size(vw, h),
                ForeColor = WHITE,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT14
            };
            parent.Controls.Add(val);
            valLabel = val;
        }
        private GroupBox MakeGroupBox(string title, int x, int y, int w, int h,
                                       Color tc, Font f)
        {
            return new GroupBox
            {
                Text = title,
                Location = new Point(x, y),
                Size = new Size(w, h),
                ForeColor = tc,
                BackColor = Color.FromArgb(12, 12, 12),
                Font = f
            };
        }
        private TrackBar DemoSlider(Control parent, string name, int min, int max,
                                     int sv, int y, out Label valueLabel)
        {
            parent.Controls.Add(new Label
            {
                Text = name,
                Location = new Point(6, y),
                Size = new Size(220, 20),
                ForeColor = Color.Silver,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT10
            });
            var vl = new Label
            {
                Text = sv.ToString(),
                Location = new Point(228, y),
                Size = new Size(148, 20),
                ForeColor = WHITE,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT11,
                TextAlign = ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft
            };
            parent.Controls.Add(vl);
            var tb = new TrackBar
            {
                Minimum = min,
                Maximum = max,
                Value = sv,
                TickFrequency = Math.Max(1, (max - min) / 10),
                SmallChange = 1,
                LargeChange = Math.Max(1, (max - min) / 20),
                Location = new Point(4, y + 22),
                Size = new Size(372, 36),
                BackColor = Color.FromArgb(30, 30, 30)
            };
            Label cap = vl;
            tb.ValueChanged += (s, ev) => cap.Text = ((TrackBar)s).Value.ToString();
            parent.Controls.Add(tb);
            valueLabel = vl;
            return tb;
        }
    }
}

        private Label _valRollAngle, _valRollCmd, _valPitchAngle, _valPitchCmd;
        private Label _valHeading, _valHeadingCmd;
        private Label _valAileron, _valFlap;
        private Label _valHMSL, _valHCmd, _valHAGL, _valRA;
        private Label _valElevator, _valROC;
        private Label _valSpeed, _valSpeedCmd, _valThrottle;
        // ── Engine & Power value labels ──────────────────────────────────
        private Label _valRPM, _valFuelMain, _valFuelLeft, _valFuelRight;
        private Label _valBattV, _valAltV, _valCHTL, _valCHTR;
        // ── Link Health value labels ─────────────────────────────────────
        private Label _valCRCFail, _valGPSMiss, _valVGMiss;
        private Label _valGPSRate, _valVGRate, _valPktNum;
        // ── Fonts & colours ──────────────────────────────────────────────
        private static readonly Font FNT14 = new Font("Consolas", 14f, FontStyle.Bold);
        private static readonly Font FNT12 = new Font("Consolas", 12f, FontStyle.Bold);
        private static readonly Font FNT11 = new Font("Consolas", 11f, FontStyle.Bold);
        private static readonly Font FNT10 = new Font("Consolas", 10f);
        private static readonly Color LIME = Color.Lime;
        private static readonly Color WHITE = Color.White;
        private static readonly Color CYAN = Color.Cyan;
        private static readonly Color BLACK = Color.Black;
        // ── Flight Block column constants ─────────────────────────────────
        private const int FL_NX = 5;
        private const int FL_NW = 137;
        private const int FL_VX = 145;
        private const int FL_VW = 95;
        private const int FL_R_NX = 250;
        private const int FL_R_NW = 105;
        private const int FL_R_VX = 350;
        private const int FL_R_VW = 130;
        private const int FL_UX = 603;
        private const int FL_H = 24;
        private const int FL_ROW = 27;
        // ── GPS section (12pt, compressed) ──────────────────────────────
        private const int GPS_ROW = 27;
        private const int GPS_H = 24;
        // ── Constructor ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
        public Form1()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
            this.Load += Form1_Load;
            this.FormClosing += Form1_FormClosing;
            BuildUI();
        }
        private void Form1_Load(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            _receiver = new PacketReceiver();
            _receiver.Open("COM11", 115200);
            _displayTimer = new System.Windows.Forms.Timer();
            _displayTimer.Interval = 100;
            _displayTimer.Tick += UpdateDisplay;
            _displayTimer.Start();
        }
        private void Form1_FormClosing(object sender, FormClosingEventArgs e)
        {
            if (_displayTimer != null) _displayTimer.Stop();
            if (_receiver != null) _receiver.Close();
        }
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  Demo toggle
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        private void BtnDemo_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            _demoMode = !_demoMode;
            if (_demoMode)
            {
                _btnDemo.Text = "DEMO  ■  ON   (click to hide sliders)";
                _btnDemo.BackColor = Color.FromArgb(0, 150, 0);
                _btnDemo.ForeColor = WHITE;
            }
            else
            {
                _btnDemo.Text = "DEMO  ▶  OFF  (click to show sliders)";
                _btnDemo.BackColor = Color.FromArgb(40, 40, 40);
                _btnDemo.ForeColor = LIME;
            }
            _pnlSliders.Visible = _demoMode;
        }
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  Display update  (100 ms timer)
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        private void UpdateDisplay(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            if (_demoMode)
            {
                _combined.Airspeed = _tbAirspeed.Value;
                _combined.Altitude = _tbAltitude.Value;
                _combined.Heading = _tbHeading.Value;
                _combined.Pitch = _tbPitch.Value;
                _combined.Roll = _tbRoll.Value;
                _combined.Refresh();
                _valRollAngle.Text = _tbRoll.Value + "°";
                _valPitchAngle.Text = _tbPitch.Value + "°";
                _valHeading.Text = _tbHeading.Value + "°";
                _valHMSL.Text = _tbAltitude.Value + " m";
                _valSpeed.Text = _tbAirspeed.Value + " m/s";
                return;
            }
            // ── Live telemetry ───────────────────────────────────────────
            byte[] p1 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[0];
            byte[] p2 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[1];
            byte[] p3 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[2];
            byte[] p5 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[4];
            byte[] p6 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[5];
            byte[] p7 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[6];
            byte[] p8 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[7];
            if (p1 == null) return;
            TelemetryData t1 = TelemetryDecoder.Decode(p1);
            _combined.Roll = (int)t1.Roll7Angle;
            _combined.Pitch = (int)t1.Pitch7Angle;
            _combined.Airspeed = (int)t1.CAS;
            _combined.Altitude = (int)t1.Hp;
            _combined.Heading = (int)t1.Heading;
            _combined.Refresh();
            _mapCtrl.UpdatePosition(t1.Latitude, t1.Longitude, t1.Heading);
            _valLat.Text = t1.Latitude.ToString("F4") + "°";
            _valLon.Text = t1.Longitude.ToString("F4") + "°";
            _valRollAngle.Text = t1.Roll7Angle.ToString("F1") + "°";
            _valRollCmd.Text = t1.Phi_Com.ToString("F1") + "°";
            _valPitchAngle.Text = t1.Pitch7Angle.ToString("F1") + "°";
            _valPitchCmd.Text = t1.Theta_Cmd.ToString("F1") + "°";
            _valHeading.Text = t1.Heading.ToString("F0") + "°";
            _valHeadingCmd.Text = t1.Psi_Com.ToString("F0") + "°";
            _valAileron.Text = t1.Inner_SB_Ail_Com.ToString("F1") + "°";
            _valFlap.Text = "N/A";
            _valHMSL.Text = t1.Hp.ToString("F0") + " m";
            _valHCmd.Text = t1.Alt_Com.ToString("F0") + " m";
            _valHAGL.Text = t1.AGL.ToString("F1") + " m";
            _valRA.Text = t1.Radar_Alt.ToString("F1") + " m";
            _valElevator.Text = t1.Top_SB_RV_Com.ToString("F1") + "°";
            _valSpeed.Text = t1.CAS.ToString("F1") + " m/s";
            _valSpeedCmd.Text = t1.CAS_Com.ToString("F1") + " m/s";
            _valThrottle.Text = (t1.Throttle_pos * 100.0).ToString("F0") + " %";
            _valRPM.Text = t1.Engine_RPM.ToString("F0") + " rpm";
            _valBattV.Text = t1.Batt_Volts.ToString("F1") + " V";
            _valAltV.Text = t1.Alt_Volts.ToString("F1") + " V";
            if (p2 != null)
            {
                TelemetryData t2 = TelemetryDecoder.Decode(p2);
                _valD2Base.Text = t2.Distance7From7Base.ToString("F1") + " km";
                _valOffTrack.Text = t2.OffTrack.ToString("F1") + " m";
                _valWP.Text = (t2.D2Go / 1000.0).ToString("F0");
            }
            if (p3 != null)
            {
                TelemetryData t3 = TelemetryDecoder.Decode(p3);
                _valROC.Text = t3.ROC_Estimated.ToString("F1") + " m/s";
            }
            if (p5 != null)
            {
                TelemetryData t5 = TelemetryDecoder.Decode(p5);
                _valGPS.Text = t5.Solution7Status > 0 ? "DIFF" : "SINGLE";
            }
            if (p6 != null)
            {
                TelemetryData t6 = TelemetryDecoder.Decode(p6);
                _valFuelMain.Text = (t6.FuelLevel_Main * 100).ToString("F0") + " %";
                _valFuelLeft.Text = (t6.FuelLevel_Left * 100).ToString("F0") + " %";
                _valFuelRight.Text = (t6.FuelLevel_Right * 100).ToString("F0") + " %";
                _valCHTL.Text = t6.CHT7Left.ToString("F0") + " °C";
                _valCHTR.Text = t6.CHT7Right.ToString("F0") + " °C";
            }
            _valCRCFail.Text = PacketReceiver.CRCFailCount.ToString();
            _valPktNum.Text = t1.PacketNumber.ToString();
            if (p7 != null)
            {
                TelemetryData t7 = TelemetryDecoder.Decode(p7);
                _valGPSMiss.Text = t7.GPSMissPacketsCount.ToString();
                _valVGMiss.Text = t7.VGMissPacketsCount.ToString();
            }
            if (p8 != null)
            {
                TelemetryData t8 = TelemetryDecoder.Decode(p8);
                _valGPSRate.Text = t8.GPSPacketRate.ToString("F0") + " pkt/s";
                _valVGRate.Text = t8.VGPacketRate.ToString("F0") + " pkt/s";
            }
        }
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  BuildUI
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        private void BuildUI()
        {
            this.Text = "GCS_240626 — Ground Control Station";
            this.ClientSize = new Size(1900, 1000);
            this.MinimumSize = new Size(1900, 1040);
            this.BackColor = BLACK;
            this.ForeColor = LIME;
            this.Font = FNT14;
            _combined = new AxCombined();
            _combined.Location = new Point(690, 10);
            _combined.Size = new Size(630, 442);
            ((System.ComponentModel.ISupportInitialize)_combined).BeginInit();
            this.Controls.Add(_combined);
            ((System.ComponentModel.ISupportInitialize)_combined).EndInit();
            BuildDemoButton();
            BuildDemoSliders();
            BuildMapPanel();
            BuildFlightBlock();
            BuildRightPanel();
        }
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  DEMO button
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        private void BuildDemoButton()
        {
            _btnDemo = new Button
            {
                //..Text = "DEMO ▶ OFF (click to show sliders)",
                Text = "DEMO",
                Location = new Point(1850, 10),
                Size = new Size(50, 30),
                BackColor = Color.FromArgb(40, 40, 40),
                ForeColor = LIME,
                Font = new Font("Consolas", 11f, FontStyle.Bold),
                FlatStyle = FlatStyle.Flat
            };
            _btnDemo.FlatAppearance.BorderColor = Color.FromArgb(0, 120, 0);
            _btnDemo.FlatAppearance.BorderSize = 1;
            _btnDemo.Click += BtnDemo_Click;
            this.Controls.Add(_btnDemo);
        }
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  DEMO slider panel
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        private void BuildDemoSliders()
        {
            _pnlSliders = new Panel
            {
                Location = new Point(690, 508),
                Size = new Size(630, 436),
                BackColor = Color.FromArgb(18, 18, 18),
                BorderStyle = BorderStyle.FixedSingle,
                Visible = false
            };
            _pnlSliders.Controls.Add(new Label
            {
                Text = "── DEMO INPUTS ──",
                Location = new Point(0, 4),
                Size = new Size(380, 22),
                ForeColor = Color.Magenta,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT11,
                TextAlign = ContentAlignment.MiddleCenter
            });
            int y = 30;
            _tbAirspeed = DemoSlider(_pnlSliders, "Airspeed (m/s)", 0, 100, 0, y, out _lblDemoAS); y += 66;
            _tbAltitude = DemoSlider(_pnlSliders, "Altitude   (m)", -1000, 11000, 0, y, out _lblDemoAlt); y += 66;
            _tbHeading = DemoSlider(_pnlSliders, "Heading  (deg)", 0, 360, 0, y, out _lblDemoHdg); y += 66;
            _tbPitch = DemoSlider(_pnlSliders, "Pitch    (deg)", -30, 30, 0, y, out _lblDemoPitch); y += 66;
            _tbRoll = DemoSlider(_pnlSliders, "Roll     (deg)", -60, 60, 0, y, out _lblDemoRoll); y += 66;
            _tbPosition = DemoSlider(_pnlSliders, "Position      ", 0, 100, 0, y, out _lblDemoPos);
            this.Controls.Add(_pnlSliders);
        }

        }
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  Flight Block
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        private void BuildFlightBlock()
        {
            var pnl = new Panel
            {
                Location = new Point(10, 10),
                Size = new Size(675, 442),
                BackColor = BLACK,
                BorderStyle = BorderStyle.FixedSingle
            };
            this.Controls.Add(pnl);
            int y = 8;
            // ── GPS / NAV ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
            FLg(pnl, "Lat:", 5, y, 58, GPS_H, LIME, ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft);
            _valLat = FLg(pnl, "----", 65, y, 100, GPS_H, WHITE, ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft);
            FLg(pnl, "D2BASE:", 163, y, 110, GPS_H, LIME, ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft);
            _valD2Base = FLg(pnl, "----", 280, y, 105, GPS_H, WHITE, ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft);
            FLg(pnl, "GPS:", 385, y, 50, GPS_H, LIME, ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft);
            _valGPS = FLg(pnl, "----", 435, y, 130, GPS_H, WHITE, ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft);
            // FLg(pnl, "[Diff/Single]", 668, y, 200, GPS_H, CYAN, ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft);
            y += GPS_ROW;
            FLg(pnl, "Lon:", 5, y, 58, GPS_H, LIME, ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft);
            _valLon = FLg(pnl, "----", 65, y, 95, GPS_H, WHITE, ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft);
            FLg(pnl, "OFFTRACK:", 163, y, 105, GPS_H, LIME, ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft);
            _valOffTrack = FLg(pnl, "----", 276, y, 110, GPS_H, WHITE, ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft);
            FLg(pnl, "WP:", 385, y, 60, GPS_H, LIME, ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft);
            _valWP = FLg(pnl, "----", 445, y, 130, GPS_H, WHITE, ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft);
            y += GPS_ROW + 3;
            Sep(pnl, 5, y, 663);
            // ── ATTITUDE ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
            y += 7;
            FL(pnl, "Sensor in Use", FL_R_NX, y, 150, FL_H, CYAN);
            FL(pnl, "[VG440]", FL_R_NX + 145, y, 120, FL_H, WHITE);
            FLn(pnl, "Roll Angle:", FL_NX, y, FL_NW, FL_H, LIME, ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft);
            _valRollAngle = FL(pnl, "----", FL_VX, y, FL_VW, FL_H, WHITE);
            y += FL_ROW;
            FLn(pnl, "Roll CMD:", FL_NX, y, FL_NW, FL_H, LIME, ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft);
            _valRollCmd = FL(pnl, "----", FL_VX, y, FL_VW, FL_H, WHITE);
            FLn(pnl, "Aileron:", FL_R_NX, y, FL_R_NW, FL_H, LIME, ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft);
            _valAileron = FL(pnl, "----", FL_R_VX, y, FL_R_VW, FL_H, WHITE);
            y += FL_ROW;
            FLn(pnl, "Pitch Angle:", FL_NX, y, FL_NW, FL_H, LIME, ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft);
            _valPitchAngle = FL(pnl, "----", FL_VX, y, FL_VW, FL_H, WHITE);
            FLn(pnl, "Flap:", FL_R_NX, y, FL_R_NW, FL_H, LIME, ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft);
            _valFlap = FL(pnl, "----", FL_R_VX, y, FL_R_VW, FL_H, WHITE);
            y += FL_ROW;
            FLn(pnl, "Pitch CMD:", FL_NX, y, FL_NW, FL_H, LIME, ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft);
            _valPitchCmd = FL(pnl, "----", FL_VX, y, FL_VW, FL_H, WHITE);
            y += FL_ROW;
            FLn(pnl, "Heading:", FL_NX, y, FL_NW, FL_H, LIME, ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft);
            _valHeading = FL(pnl, "----", FL_VX, y, FL_VW, FL_H, WHITE);

            _valHeadingCmd = FL(pnl, "----", FL_VX, y, FL_VW, FL_H, WHITE);

            // ── HEIGHT ───────────────────────────────────────────────────

        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  Right column: Engine & Power + Link Health
        //  ROW=24, H=24 → last ENGINE row bottom = 34 + 7×24 + 24 = 226
        //  ENGINE height = 230  (226 + 4 margin)
        //  LINK y        = 10 + 230 + 6 = 246
        //  LINK last row bottom = 34 + 5×24 + 24 = 178
        //  LINK height   = 182  (178 + 4 margin)
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        private void BuildRightPanel()
        {
            const int ROW = 24, H = 24, NX = 8, NW = 130, VX = 142, VW = 300;
            var grpEng = MakeGroupBox("ENGINE & POWER", 1330, 10, 452, 230, Color.Orange, FNT14);
            int y = 34;
            EngRow(grpEng, "RPM:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valRPM); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpEng, "Fuel Main:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valFuelMain); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpEng, "Fuel Left:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valFuelLeft); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpEng, "Fuel Right:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valFuelRight); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpEng, "Batt V:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valBattV); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpEng, "Alt V:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valAltV); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpEng, "CHT Left:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valCHTL); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpEng, "CHT Right:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valCHTR);
            this.Controls.Add(grpEng);
            var grpLink = MakeGroupBox("LINK HEALTH", 1330, 240, 452, 180, Color.Yellow, FNT14);
            y = 34;
            EngRow(grpLink, "CRC Fails:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valCRCFail); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpLink, "GPS Miss:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valGPSMiss); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpLink, "VG Miss:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valVGMiss); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpLink, "GPS Rate:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valGPSRate); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpLink, "VG Rate:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valVGRate); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpLink, "Last Pkt #:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valPktNum);
            this.Controls.Add(grpLink);
        }
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  Helpers
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        private Label FL(Control p, string t, int x, int y, int w, int h, Color fg)
        {
            var l = new Label
            {
                Text = t,
                Location = new Point(x, y),
                Size = new Size(w, h),
                ForeColor = fg,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT14
            };
            p.Controls.Add(l);
            return l;
        }
        private Label FLn(Control p, string t, int x, int y, int w, int h,
                           Color fg, ContentAlignment a)
        {
            var l = new Label
            {
                Text = t,
                Location = new Point(x, y),
                Size = new Size(w, h),
                ForeColor = fg,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT14,
                TextAlign = a
            };
            p.Controls.Add(l);
            return l;
        }
        private Label FLg(Control p, string t, int x, int y, int w, int h,
                           Color fg, ContentAlignment a)
        {
            var l = new Label
            {
                Text = t,
                Location = new Point(x, y),
                Size = new Size(w, h),
                ForeColor = fg,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT14,
                TextAlign = a
            };
            p.Controls.Add(l);
            return l;
        }
        private void Sep(Control p, int x, int y, int w)
        {
            p.Controls.Add(new Panel
            {
                Location = new Point(x, y),
                Size = new Size(w, 2),
                BackColor = Color.FromArgb(0, 140, 0)
            });
        }
        private void EngRow(Control parent, string name, int nx, int y, int nw, int h,
                             int vx, int vw, out Label valLabel)
        {
            parent.Controls.Add(new Label
            {
                Text = name,
                Location = new Point(nx, y),
                Size = new Size(nw, h),
                ForeColor = LIME,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT14,
                TextAlign = ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft
            });
            var val = new Label
            {
                Text = "----",
                Location = new Point(vx, y),
                Size = new Size(vw, h),
                ForeColor = WHITE,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT14
            };
            parent.Controls.Add(val);
            valLabel = val;
        }
        private GroupBox MakeGroupBox(string title, int x, int y, int w, int h,
                                       Color tc, Font f)
        {
            return new GroupBox
            {
                Text = title,
                Location = new Point(x, y),
                Size = new Size(w, h),
                ForeColor = tc,
                BackColor = Color.FromArgb(12, 12, 12),
                Font = f
            };
        }
        private TrackBar DemoSlider(Control parent, string name, int min, int max,
                                     int sv, int y, out Label valueLabel)
        {
            parent.Controls.Add(new Label
            {
                Text = name,
                Location = new Point(6, y),
                Size = new Size(220, 20),
                ForeColor = Color.Silver,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT10
            });
            var vl = new Label
            {
                Text = sv.ToString(),
                Location = new Point(228, y),
                Size = new Size(148, 20),
                ForeColor = WHITE,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT11,
                TextAlign = ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft
            };
            parent.Controls.Add(vl);
            var tb = new TrackBar
            {
                Minimum = min,
                Maximum = max,
                Value = sv,
                TickFrequency = Math.Max(1, (max - min) / 10),
                SmallChange = 1,
                LargeChange = Math.Max(1, (max - min) / 20),
                Location = new Point(4, y + 22),
                Size = new Size(372, 36),
                BackColor = Color.FromArgb(30, 30, 30)
            };
            Label cap = vl;
            tb.ValueChanged += (s, ev) => cap.Text = ((TrackBar)s).Value.ToString();
            parent.Controls.Add(tb);
            valueLabel = vl;
            return tb;
        }
    }
}

sync... using System;
using System.Drawing;

// ============================================================
//  Form1.cs  –  GCS_240626

//  Font    : Consolas 14pt Bold, Neon Green on Black
//
//  Layout
//  ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
//   x=10   PFD (384×372)           │  MAP (1010×452)    │  ENGINE (455×295)
//   x=10   [DEMO btn] (384×40)     │                    │  LINK   (455×230)
//   x=10   [DEMO sliders — hidden] │                    │
//   ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
//          FLIGHT BLOCK (1010×522)  bottom-centre
//
//  Demo behaviour
//  ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
//  • "DEMO ▶ OFF" button is ALWAYS visible below the PFD.
//  • Click once  → slider panel appears, demo mode ON.
//  • Click again → slider panel hides, live mode resumes.
// ============================================================
namespace GCS_240626
{
    public partial class Form1 : Form
    {
        // ── Serial & timer ───────────────────────────────────────────────
        private PacketReceiver _receiver;
        private System.Windows.Forms.Timer _displayTimer;
        // ── Controls ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
        private AxCombined _combined;
        private MapControl _mapCtrl;
        // ── Demo ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
        private bool _demoMode = false;
        private Button _btnDemo;          // always visible
        private Panel _pnlSliders;       // hidden until DEMO ON
        private TrackBar _tbAirspeed, _tbAltitude, _tbHeading, _tbPitch, _tbRoll, _tbPosition;
        private Label _lblDemoAS, _lblDemoAlt, _lblDemoHdg, _lblDemoPitch, _lblDemoRoll, _lblDemoPos;
        // ── Flight block value labels ─────────────────────────────────────
        private Label _valLat, _valLon, _valD2Base, _valOffTrack, _valGPS, _valWP;
        private Label _valRollAngle, _valRollCmd, _valPitchAngle, _valPitchCmd;
        private Label _valHeading, _valHeadingCmd;
        private Label _valAileron, _valFlap;
        private Label _valHMSL, _valHCmd, _valHAGL, _valRA;
        private Label _valElevator, _valROC;
        private Label _valSpeed, _valSpeedCmd, _valThrottle;
        // ── Engine & Power value labels ──────────────────────────────────
        private Label _valRPM, _valFuelMain, _valFuelLeft, _valFuelRight;
        private Label _valBattV, _valAltV, _valCHTL, _valCHTR;
        // ── Link Health value labels ─────────────────────────────────────
        private Label _valCRCFail, _valGPSMiss, _valVGMiss;
        private Label _valGPSRate, _valVGRate, _valPktNum;
        // ── Fonts & colours ──────────────────────────────────────────────
        private static readonly Font FNT14 = new Font("Consolas", 14f, FontStyle.Bold);
        private static readonly Font FNT12 = new Font("Consolas", 12f, FontStyle.Bold);
        private static readonly Font FNT11 = new Font("Consolas", 11f, FontStyle.Bold);
        private static readonly Font FNT10 = new Font("Consolas", 10f);
        private static readonly Color LIME = Color.Lime;
        private static readonly Color WHITE = Color.White;
        private static readonly Color CYAN = Color.Cyan;
        private static readonly Color BLACK = Color.Black;
        // ── Flight Block column constants ─────────────────────────────────
        private const int FL_NX = 5;
        private const int FL_NW = 137;
        private const int FL_VX = 145;
        private const int FL_VW = 95;
        private const int FL_R_NX = 250;
        private const int FL_R_NW = 105;
        private const int FL_R_VX = 350;
        private const int FL_R_VW = 130;
        private const int FL_UX = 603;
        private const int FL_H = 24;
        private const int FL_ROW = 27;

        private const int GPS_H = 24;
        // ── Constructor ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
        public Form1()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
            this.Load += Form1_Load;
            this.FormClosing += Form1_FormClosing;
            BuildUI();

        private void Form1_Load(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            _receiver = new PacketReceiver();
            _receiver.Open("COM11", 115200);
            _displayTimer = new System.Windows.Forms.Timer();
            _displayTimer.Interval = 100;
            _displayTimer.Tick += UpdateDisplay;
            _displayTimer.Start();
        }
        private void Form1_FormClosing(object sender, FormClosingEventArgs e)
        {
            if (_displayTimer != null) _displayTimer.Stop();
            if (_receiver != null) _receiver.Close();
        }
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  Demo toggle
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        private void BtnDemo_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            _demoMode = !_demoMode;
            if (_demoMode)
            {
                _btnDemo.Text = "DEMO  ■  ON   (click to hide sliders)";
                _btnDemo.BackColor = Color.FromArgb(0, 150, 0);
                _btnDemo.ForeColor = WHITE;
            }
            else
            {
                _btnDemo.Text = "DEMO  ▶  OFF  (click to show sliders)";
                _btnDemo.BackColor = Color.FromArgb(40, 40, 40);
                _btnDemo.ForeColor = LIME;
            }
            _pnlSliders.Visible = _demoMode;
        }
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  Display update  (100 ms timer)
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        private void UpdateDisplay(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            if (_demoMode)
            {
                _combined.Airspeed = _tbAirspeed.Value;
                _combined.Altitude = _tbAltitude.Value;
                _combined.Heading = _tbHeading.Value;
                _combined.Pitch = _tbPitch.Value;
                _combined.Roll = _tbRoll.Value;
                _combined.Refresh();
                _valRollAngle.Text = _tbRoll.Value + "°";
                _valPitchAngle.Text = _tbPitch.Value + "°";
                _valHeading.Text = _tbHeading.Value + "°";
                _valHMSL.Text = _tbAltitude.Value + " m";
                _valSpeed.Text = _tbAirspeed.Value + " m/s";
                return;
            }
            // ── Live telemetry ───────────────────────────────────────────
            byte[] p1 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[0];
            byte[] p2 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[1];
            byte[] p3 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[2];
            byte[] p5 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[4];
            byte[] p6 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[5];
            byte[] p7 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[6];
            byte[] p8 = PacketReceiver.PacketData[7];
            if (p1 == null) return;
            TelemetryData t1 = TelemetryDecoder.Decode(p1);
            _combined.Roll = (int)t1.Roll7Angle;
            _combined.Pitch = (int)t1.Pitch7Angle;
            _combined.Airspeed = (int)t1.CAS;
            _combined.Altitude = (int)t1.Hp;
            _combined.Heading = (int)t1.Heading;
            _combined.Refresh();
            _mapCtrl.UpdatePosition(t1.Latitude, t1.Longitude, t1.Heading);
            _valLat.Text = t1.Latitude.ToString("F4") + "°";
            _valLon.Text = t1.Longitude.ToString("F4") + "°";
            _valRollAngle.Text = t1.Roll7Angle.ToString("F1") + "°";
            _valRollCmd.Text = t1.Phi_Com.ToString("F1") + "°";
            _valPitchAngle.Text = t1.Pitch7Angle.ToString("F1") + "°";
            _valPitchCmd.Text = t1.Theta_Cmd.ToString("F1") + "°";
            _valHeading.Text = t1.Heading.ToString("F0") + "°";
            _valHeadingCmd.Text = t1.Psi_Com.ToString("F0") + "°";
            _valAileron.Text = t1.Inner_SB_Ail_Com.ToString("F1") + "°";
            _valFlap.Text = "N/A";
            _valHMSL.Text = t1.Hp.ToString("F0") + " m";
            _valHCmd.Text = t1.Alt_Com.ToString("F0") + " m";
            _valHAGL.Text = t1.AGL.ToString("F1") + " m";
            _valRA.Text = t1.Radar_Alt.ToString("F1") + " m";
            _valElevator.Text = t1.Top_SB_RV_Com.ToString("F1") + "°";
            _valSpeed.Text = t1.CAS.ToString("F1") + " m/s";
            _valSpeedCmd.Text = t1.CAS_Com.ToString("F1") + " m/s";
            _valThrottle.Text = (t1.Throttle_pos * 100.0).ToString("F0") + " %";
            _valRPM.Text = t1.Engine_RPM.ToString("F0") + " rpm";
            _valBattV.Text = t1.Batt_Volts.ToString("F1") + " V";
            _valAltV.Text = t1.Alt_Volts.ToString("F1") + " V";
            if (p2 != null)
            {
                TelemetryData t2 = TelemetryDecoder.Decode(p2);
                _valD2Base.Text = t2.Distance7From7Base.ToString("F1") + " km";
                _valOffTrack.Text = t2.OffTrack.ToString("F1") + " m";
                _valWP.Text = (t2.D2Go / 1000.0).ToString("F0");
            }
            if (p3 != null)
            {
                TelemetryData t3 = TelemetryDecoder.Decode(p3);
                _valROC.Text = t3.ROC_Estimated.ToString("F1") + " m/s";
            }
            if (p5 != null)
            {
                TelemetryData t5 = TelemetryDecoder.Decode(p5);
                _valGPS.Text = t5.Solution7Status > 0 ? "DIFF" : "SINGLE";
            }
            if (p6 != null)
            {
                TelemetryData t6 = TelemetryDecoder.Decode(p6);
                _valFuelMain.Text = (t6.FuelLevel_Main * 100).ToString("F0") + " %";
                _valFuelLeft.Text = (t6.FuelLevel_Left * 100).ToString("F0") + " %";
                _valFuelRight.Text = (t6.FuelLevel_Right * 100).ToString("F0") + " %";
                _valCHTL.Text = t6.CHT7Left.ToString("F0") + " °C";
                _valCHTR.Text = t6.CHT7Right.ToString("F0") + " °C";
            }
            _valCRCFail.Text = PacketReceiver.CRCFailCount.ToString();
            _valPktNum.Text = t1.PacketNumber.ToString();
            if (p7 != null)
            {
                TelemetryData t7 = TelemetryDecoder.Decode(p7);
                _valGPSMiss.Text = t7.GPSMissPacketsCount.ToString();
                _valVGMiss.Text = t7.VGMissPacketsCount.ToString();
            }
            if (p8 != null)
            {
                TelemetryData t8 = TelemetryDecoder.Decode(p8);
                _valGPSRate.Text = t8.GPSPacketRate.ToString("F0") + " pkt/s";
                _valVGRate.Text = t8.VGPacketRate.ToString("F0") + " pkt/s";
            }
        }

            this.Text = "GCS_240626 — Ground Control Station";

            this.MinimumSize = new Size(1900, 1040);

            this.ForeColor = LIME;
            this.Font = FNT14;

            ((System.ComponentModel.ISupportInitialize)_combined).BeginInit();
            this.Controls.Add(_combined);
            ((System.ComponentModel.ISupportInitialize)_combined).EndInit();
            BuildDemoButton();
            BuildDemoSliders();
            BuildMapPanel();
            BuildFlightBlock();
            BuildRightPanel();
            BuildSidePanels();
        }

        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  Right column: Engine & Power + Link Health
        //  ROW=24, H=24 → last ENGINE row bottom = 34 + 7×24 + 24 = 226
        //  ENGINE height = 230  (226 + 4 margin)
        //  LINK y        = 10 + 230 + 6 = 246
        //  LINK last row bottom = 34 + 5×24 + 24 = 178
        //  LINK height   = 182  (178 + 4 margin)
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  Side button panels — left and right of the PFD
        //  Left  panel : x=592, w=96  (gap between FlightBlock x+w=590 and PFD x=690)
        //  Right panel : x=1222, w=106 (gap between PFD x+w=1220 and ENGINE x=1330)
        //  Both share same height as PFD (h=442). Buttons: 80×55, 6 rows, centred.
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        private void BuildSidePanels()
        {
            const int PNL_H = 442;
            const int BW = 80, BH = 55, V_GAP = 8, TOP = 8;
            const int ROWS = 6;   // floor((442-16)/(55+8)) = 6
            // ── Left panel ───────────────────────────────────────────────
            var pnlL = new Panel
            {
                Location = new Point(592, 10),
                Size = new Size(96, PNL_H),
                BackColor = Color.FromArgb(12, 12, 12),
                BorderStyle = BorderStyle.FixedSingle
            };
            int lbx = (96 - BW) / 2;   // = 8
            for (int r = 0; r < ROWS; r++)
            {
                int by = TOP + r * (BH + V_GAP);
                pnlL.Controls.Add(new GcsButton
                {
                    Text = $"L{r + 1}",
                    Location = new Point(lbx, by),
                    Size = new Size(BW, BH),
                    ForeColor = LIME,
                    Font = FNT11
                });
            }
            this.Controls.Add(pnlL);
            // ── Right panel ──────────────────────────────────────────────
            var pnlR = new Panel
            {
                Location = new Point(1222, 10),
                Size = new Size(106, PNL_H),
                BackColor = Color.FromArgb(12, 12, 12),
                BorderStyle = BorderStyle.FixedSingle
            };
            int rbx = (106 - BW) / 2;  // = 13
            for (int r = 0; r < ROWS; r++)
            {
                int by = TOP + r * (BH + V_GAP);
                pnlR.Controls.Add(new GcsButton
                {
                    Text = $"R{r + 1}",
                    Location = new Point(rbx, by),
                    Size = new Size(BW, BH),
                    ForeColor = LIME,
                    Font = FNT11
                });
            }
            this.Controls.Add(pnlR);
        }
        private void BuildRightPanel()
        {
            const int ROW = 24, H = 24, NX = 8, NW = 130, VX = 142, VW = 100;
            const int PANEL_W = 245;   // VX + VW + 3 margin
            var grpEng = MakeGroupBox("ENGINE & POWER", 1330, 10, PANEL_W, 230, Color.Orange, FNT14);
            int y = 34;
            EngRow(grpEng, "RPM:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valRPM); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpEng, "Fuel Main:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valFuelMain); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpEng, "Fuel Left:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valFuelLeft); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpEng, "Fuel Right:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valFuelRight); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpEng, "Batt V:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valBattV); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpEng, "Alt V:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valAltV); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpEng, "CHT Left:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valCHTL); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpEng, "CHT Right:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valCHTR);
            this.Controls.Add(grpEng);
            var grpLink = MakeGroupBox("LINK HEALTH", 1330, 240, PANEL_W, 180, Color.Yellow, FNT14);
            y = 34;
            EngRow(grpLink, "CRC Fails:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valCRCFail); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpLink, "GPS Miss:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valGPSMiss); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpLink, "VG Miss:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valVGMiss); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpLink, "GPS Rate:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valGPSRate); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpLink, "VG Rate:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valVGRate); y += ROW;
            EngRow(grpLink, "Last Pkt #:", NX, y, NW, H, VX, VW, out _valPktNum);
            this.Controls.Add(grpLink);
            // ── Command Tabs (below LINK HEALTH) ─────────────────────────
            BuildCommandTabs();
        }
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  Command Tab Panel  (x=1330, below LINK HEALTH at y=424)
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        private void BuildCommandTabs()
        {
            // TabControl spans x=1330 to right screen edge (1900-10=1890)
            var tc = new TabControl
            {
                Location = new Point(1450, 424),
                Size = new Size(460, 566),
                Font = FNT11,
                Appearance = TabAppearance.Normal,
                Alignment = TabAlignment.Bottom,
                DrawMode = TabDrawMode.OwnerDrawFixed,
                ItemSize = new Size(84, 28),   // tab strip: width per tab, height of strip
                Padding = new Point(6, 4)
            };
            // ── Owner-draw: 3-D beveled tab headers ─────────────────────
            tc.DrawItem += (sender, ev) =>
            {
                var tab = (TabControl)sender;
                bool sel = (tab.SelectedIndex == ev.Index);
                var g = ev.Graphics;
                var r = ev.Bounds;
                Color face = sel ? Color.FromArgb(65, 65, 65) : Color.FromArgb(22, 22, 22);
                Color hi = Color.FromArgb(125, 125, 125);
                Color sh = Color.FromArgb(10, 10, 10);
                Color fg = sel ? Color.Lime : Color.FromArgb(90, 140, 90);
                // Fill face
                g.FillRectangle(new SolidBrush(face), r);
                // 3-D bevel (2-pixel) — bottom-aligned tabs:
                //   selected   → highlight on bottom + sides (raised toward viewer)
                //   unselected → shadow on sides, soft highlight on bottom (recessed)
                const int B = 2;
                if (sel)
                {
                    using (var p = new Pen(hi, 1))
                    {
                        for (int i = 0; i < B; i++)
                        {
                            g.DrawLine(p, r.Left + i, r.Top, r.Left + i, r.Bottom - 1 - i);
                            g.DrawLine(p, r.Left + i, r.Bottom - 1 - i, r.Right - 1 - i, r.Bottom - 1 - i);
                            g.DrawLine(p, r.Right - 1 - i, r.Top, r.Right - 1 - i, r.Bottom - 1 - i);
                        }
                    }
                }
                else
                {
                    using (var pHi = new Pen(hi, 1))
                    using (var pSh = new Pen(sh, 1))
                    {
                        for (int i = 0; i < B; i++)
                        {
                            g.DrawLine(pSh, r.Left + i, r.Top, r.Left + i, r.Bottom - 1 - i);
                            g.DrawLine(pHi, r.Left + i, r.Bottom - 1 - i, r.Right - 1 - i, r.Bottom - 1 - i);
                            g.DrawLine(pSh, r.Right - 1 - i, r.Top, r.Right - 1 - i, r.Bottom - 1 - i);
                        }
                    }
                }
                // Centred label
                var fmt = new StringFormat
                {
                    Alignment = StringAlignment.Center,
                    LineAlignment = StringAlignment.Center
                };
                g.DrawString(tab.TabPages[ev.Index].Text, tab.Font,
                             new SolidBrush(fg), r, fmt);
            };
            string[] tabNames = { "Tab1", "Tab2", "Tab3", "Tab4", "Tab5" };
            string[][] btnLabels =
            {
                new[] { "Btn01","Btn02","Btn03","Btn04", "Btn05","Btn06","Btn07","Btn08",
                        "Btn09","Btn10","Btn11","Btn12", "Btn13","Btn14","Btn15","Btn16",
                        "Btn17","Btn18","Btn19","Btn20" },
                new[] { "Btn01","Btn02","Btn03","Btn04", "Btn05","Btn06","Btn07","Btn08",
                        "Btn09","Btn10","Btn11","Btn12", "Btn13","Btn14","Btn15","Btn16",
                        "Btn17","Btn18","Btn19","Btn20" },
                new[] { "Btn01","Btn02","Btn03","Btn04", "Btn05","Btn06","Btn07","Btn08",
                        "Btn09","Btn10","Btn11","Btn12", "Btn13","Btn14","Btn15","Btn16",
                        "Btn17","Btn18","Btn19","Btn20" },
                new[] { "Btn01","Btn02","Btn03","Btn04", "Btn05","Btn06","Btn07","Btn08",
                        "Btn09","Btn10","Btn11","Btn12", "Btn13","Btn14","Btn15","Btn16",
                        "Btn17","Btn18","Btn19","Btn20" },
                new[] { "Btn01","Btn02","Btn03","Btn04", "Btn05","Btn06","Btn07","Btn08",
                        "Btn09","Btn10","Btn11","Btn12", "Btn13","Btn14","Btn15","Btn16",
                        "Btn17","Btn18","Btn19","Btn20" },
            };
            // Grid constants
            const int COLS = 4;
            const int BW = 80, BH = 70;
            const int H_GAP = 27;   // (454 − 4×80) / 5  ≈ equal spacing
            const int V_GAP = 10;
            const int START_Y = 12;
            const int ROW_STRIDE = BH + V_GAP;   // 80 px per row
            const int FILLED_ROWS = 5;            // 6 rows fit; last left empty
            for (int t = 0; t < tabNames.Length; t++)
            {
                var page = new TabPage(tabNames[t])
                {
                    BackColor = Color.FromArgb(12, 12, 12),
                    ForeColor = LIME
                };
                int idx = 0;
                for (int row = 0; row < FILLED_ROWS; row++)
                {
                    int by = START_Y + row * ROW_STRIDE;
                    for (int col = 0; col < COLS; col++)
                    {
                        int bx = H_GAP + col * (BW + H_GAP);
                        var btn = new GcsButton
                        {
                            Text = btnLabels[t][idx++],
                            Location = new Point(bx, by),
                            Size = new Size(BW, BH),
                            ForeColor = LIME,
                            Font = FNT11
                        };
                        page.Controls.Add(btn);
                    }
                }
                tc.TabPages.Add(page);
            }
            this.Controls.Add(tc);
        }
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  Helpers
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        private Label FL(Control p, string t, int x, int y, int w, int h, Color fg)
        {
            var l = new Label
            {
                Text = t,
                Location = new Point(x, y),
                Size = new Size(w, h),
                ForeColor = fg,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT14
            };
            p.Controls.Add(l);
            return l;
        }
        private Label FLn(Control p, string t, int x, int y, int w, int h,
                           Color fg, ContentAlignment a)
        {
            var l = new Label
            {
                Text = t,
                Location = new Point(x, y),
                Size = new Size(w, h),
                ForeColor = fg,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT14,
                TextAlign = a
            };
            p.Controls.Add(l);
            return l;
        }
        private Label FLg(Control p, string t, int x, int y, int w, int h,
                           Color fg, ContentAlignment a)
        {
            var l = new Label
            {
                Text = t,
                Location = new Point(x, y),
                Size = new Size(w, h),
                ForeColor = fg,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT14,
                TextAlign = a
            };
            p.Controls.Add(l);
            return l;
        }
        private void Sep(Control p, int x, int y, int w)
        {
            p.Controls.Add(new Panel
            {
                Location = new Point(x, y),
                Size = new Size(w, 2),
                BackColor = Color.FromArgb(0, 140, 0)
            });
        }
        private void EngRow(Control parent, string name, int nx, int y, int nw, int h,
                             int vx, int vw, out Label valLabel)
        {
            parent.Controls.Add(new Label
            {
                Text = name,
                Location = new Point(nx, y),
                Size = new Size(nw, h),
                ForeColor = LIME,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT14,
                TextAlign = ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft
            });
            var val = new Label
            {
                Text = "----",
                Location = new Point(vx, y),
                Size = new Size(vw, h),
                ForeColor = WHITE,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT14
            };
            parent.Controls.Add(val);
            valLabel = val;
        }
        private GroupBox MakeGroupBox(string title, int x, int y, int w, int h,
                                       Color tc, Font f)
        {
            return new GroupBox
            {
                Text = title,
                Location = new Point(x, y),
                Size = new Size(w, h),
                ForeColor = tc,
                BackColor = Color.FromArgb(12, 12, 12),
                Font = f
            };
        }
        private TrackBar DemoSlider(Control parent, string name, int min, int max,
                                     int sv, int y, out Label valueLabel)
        {
            parent.Controls.Add(new Label
            {
                Text = name,
                Location = new Point(6, y),
                Size = new Size(220, 20),
                ForeColor = Color.Silver,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT10
            });
            var vl = new Label
            {
                Text = sv.ToString(),
                Location = new Point(228, y),
                Size = new Size(148, 20),
                ForeColor = WHITE,
                BackColor = Color.Transparent,
                Font = FNT11,
                TextAlign = ContentAlignment.MiddleLeft
            };
            parent.Controls.Add(vl);
            var tb = new TrackBar
            {
                Minimum = min,
                Maximum = max,
                Value = sv,
                TickFrequency = Math.Max(1, (max - min) / 10),
                SmallChange = 1,
                LargeChange = Math.Max(1, (max - min) / 20),
                Location = new Point(4, y + 22),
                Size = new Size(372, 36),
                BackColor = Color.FromArgb(30, 30, 30)
            };
            Label cap = vl;
            tb.ValueChanged += (s, ev) => cap.Text = ((TrackBar)s).Value.ToString();
            parent.Controls.Add(tb);
            valueLabel = vl;
            return tb;
        }
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  GcsButton — beveled panel-style toggle button
        //  First click → latches ON (sunken, green).
        //  Second click → releases OFF (raised, dark grey).
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        private class GcsButton : Button
        {
            private bool _isOn = false;  // latched toggle state
            private bool _mouseHeld = false;  // transient hold visual
            private static readonly Color CLR_OFF = Color.FromArgb(55, 55, 55);
            private static readonly Color CLR_ON = Color.FromArgb(0, 130, 0);
            private static readonly Color CLR_HI = Color.FromArgb(130, 130, 130);
            private static readonly Color CLR_SH = Color.FromArgb(15, 15, 15);
            public bool IsOn => _isOn;
            public GcsButton()
            {
                SetStyle(ControlStyles.UserPaint |
                         ControlStyles.AllPaintingInWmPaint |
                         ControlStyles.DoubleBuffer, true);
            }
            protected override void OnMouseDown(MouseEventArgs e)
            {
                _mouseHeld = true;
                Invalidate();
                base.OnMouseDown(e);
            }
            protected override void OnMouseUp(MouseEventArgs e)
            {
                _mouseHeld = false;
                _isOn = !_isOn;   // latch / unlatch on release
                Invalidate();
                base.OnMouseUp(e);
            }
            protected override void OnMouseLeave(EventArgs e)
            {
                if (_mouseHeld) { _mouseHeld = false; Invalidate(); }
                base.OnMouseLeave(e);
            }
            protected override void OnPaint(PaintEventArgs e)
            {
                // Show pressed look while held OR while latched ON
                bool showPressed = _isOn || _mouseHeld;
                var g = e.Graphics;
                var r = ClientRectangle;
                const int B = 3;
                g.FillRectangle(new SolidBrush(showPressed ? CLR_ON : CLR_OFF), r);
                Color hi = showPressed ? CLR_SH : CLR_HI;
                Color sh = showPressed ? CLR_HI : CLR_SH;
                using (var pHi = new Pen(hi, 1))
                using (var pSh = new Pen(sh, 1))
                {
                    for (int i = 0; i < B; i++)
                    {
                        g.DrawLine(pHi, i, i, r.Width - 1 - i, i);
                        g.DrawLine(pHi, i, i, i, r.Height - 1 - i);
                        g.DrawLine(pSh, i, r.Height - 1 - i, r.Width - 1 - i, r.Height - 1 - i);
                        g.DrawLine(pSh, r.Width - 1 - i, i, r.Width - 1 - i, r.Height - 1 - i);
                    }
                }
                int d = showPressed ? 1 : 0;
                var fmt = new StringFormat
                {
                    Alignment = StringAlignment.Center,
                    LineAlignment = StringAlignment.Center
                };
                g.DrawString(Text, Font, new SolidBrush(ForeColor),
                             new RectangleF(r.X + d, r.Y + d, r.Width, r.Height), fmt);
            }
        }
    }
}

   - Make3DPanel (critical — correct docking order):
     ```csharp
     private Panel Make3DPanel(Control content)
     {
         var border = new Panel
         {
             Dock      = DockStyle.Left,
             Width     = TAB_ROW_W + 10,
             BackColor = Color.FromArgb(200, 200, 200),
             Padding   = new Padding(5, 5, 5, 0)
         };
         // Fill content added FIRST (lower index)
         content.Dock = DockStyle.Fill;
         border.Controls.Add(content);
         // Bottom border added LAST (higher index = processed first by docking)
         border.Controls.Add(new Panel
         {
             Dock      = DockStyle.Bottom,
             Height    = 5,
             BackColor = Color.FromArgb(200, 200, 200)
         });
         return border;
     }
     ```
   - BuildBottomStrip:
     ```csharp
     int halfW = TAB_NW + 1 + TAB_VW;
     // Gap between tab and bottom strip
     this.Controls.Add(new Panel { Dock=DockStyle.Bottom, Height=10, BackColor=BLACK });
     var pnlStrip = new Panel
     {
         Dock=DockStyle.Bottom, Height=BOT_H,
         BackColor=Color.FromArgb(200,200,200), Padding=new Padding(5)
     };
     var pnlStripInner = new Panel { Dock=DockStyle.Fill, BackColor=BLACK };
     var pnlLeft = BuildBottomHalf(leftNames, halfW);
     pnlLeft.Location = new Point(0, 0);
     var pnlRight = BuildBottomHalf(rightNames, halfW);
     pnlRight.Location = new Point(halfW + 2, 0);
     pnlStripInner.Controls.Add(pnlLeft);
     pnlStripInner.Controls.Add(pnlRight);
     pnlStrip.Controls.Add(pnlStripInner);
     this.Controls.Add(pnlStrip);
     ```

4. Errors and Fixes:
   - **Even distribution not in synced code**: User's pasted version still had TOP=8, V_GAP=8. Applied computed vGap formula.
   - **Form2 too big**: FormBorderStyle.None → Sizable adds title bar to Size. Fix: WindowState=Maximized.
   - **Tab control not filling**: Dock=Fill not set initially. Fixed with Dock=DockStyle.Fill.
   - **White background in bottom right**: TableLayoutPanel BackColor was transparent. Fixed by setting BLACK on TableLayoutPanel and half-panels.
   - **Border around entire screen**: Used tcWrapper with Dock=Fill which put border around the whole form. User explicitly said "You are making a boundary around the screen, not around tabs." Fixed by removing tcWrapper and making Make3DPanel use Dock=Left so border only wraps the NAME/VALUE column.
   - **Paint event border invisible**: Paint fires behind child controls. Fixed by using BackColor border approach (parent BackColor = gray, Padding reveals it).
   - **Bottom border line missing**: Docking order bug. Dock=Bottom panel added BEFORE Dock=Fill content meant Fill took all space first. Fix: add Fill content first (lower z-index), then add Dock=Bottom panel last (higher z-index = processed first in layout).

5. Problem Solving:
   - WinForms docking order is critical: for Dock=Bottom + Dock=Fill in same container, the Dock=Bottom control must be added AFTER the Dock=Fill control (higher Controls index = processed first in layout).
   - BackColor border technique: reliable alternative to Paint events when child controls would cover painted borders.
   - Make3DPanel uses Dock=Left (not Dock=Fill) so the border only surrounds the NAME/VALUE content, leaving area 4 (right portion of tab) free for future controls.
   - TextRenderer.MeasureText used for precise column sizing at runtime, accounting for actual system DPI and font rendering.

[497] CLAUDE
----------------------------------------
The fix is in. Here's what changed in `Make3DPanel`:

**Old approach** (broken): single panel with `BackColor`+`Padding` for 3 sides, then one explicit bottom panel — but the TabControl's own frame was eating that bottom panel's space.

**New approach**: four explicit border panels (Top/Left/Right/Bottom), each a separate `Panel` with `Dock` set. The key is the **add order**:
- `content` added **first** (index 0) → processed last → fills the inner area
- Top/Left/Right added next
- Bottom added **last** (highest index) → processed first by WinForms layout → **always claims its 5px before anything else**

This makes the bottom border independent of the TabControl frame — it will always be visible.

[549] USER

[550] CLAUDE
----------------------------------------
These are **commented-out MFC C++ lines** (Visual Studio MFC framework).

`m_wndPropList` is a `CMFCPropertyGridCtrl` — a property grid control (the kind you see in Visual Studio's Properties panel). The two lines together would have:

1. Retrieved the property at **index 1** from the grid, with a comment suggesting it corresponds to a property named `DispDnum`
2. Set that property's displayed value to the string `"5"`

The `//` comments mean they were disabled — probably debugging code or a test someone wrote to force-set a value programmatically, then commented out rather than deleted. The `_T("5")` macro wraps the string for Unicode/MBCS compatibility, standard in MFC.

[551] USER
----------------------------------------
what it does.. if (!WriteFile(SimData.handleTel, Tel_Frame, BYTEsToWrite, NULL, &osWrite))

[552] CLAUDE
----------------------------------------
This is a **Windows API `WriteFile` call** for **asynchronous (overlapped) serial port writing**.

Breaking it down:

`WriteFile(SimData.handleTel, Tel_Frame, BYTEsToWrite, NULL, &osWrite)`

- `SimData.handleTel` — the handle to an open serial port (or file/pipe)
- `Tel_Frame` — the buffer containing the data to write (your telemetry frame)
- `BYTEsToWrite` — how many bytes to send
- `NULL` — instead of a `DWORD*` for bytes written, NULL is passed here, which is only valid for **overlapped (async) I/O**
- `&osWrite` — pointer to an `OVERLAPPED` structure, confirming this is async

The `if (!...)` means: **if the write fails**, execute the error-handling block. But with overlapped I/O, `WriteFile` returning `FALSE` doesn't always mean failure — you'd then check `GetLastError()` for `ERROR_IO_PENDING`, which means the write was queued successfully and will complete asynchronously. True failure is any other error code.

In short: it's sending a telemetry frame out the serial port asynchronously, and the `if` block catches either a real write error or handles the pending state.

2. Key Technical Concepts:
   - WinForms programmatic layout (.NET Framework 4.8), no Designer
   - WinForms docking order: controls added LAST have highest z-index → processed FIRST by layout engine
   - Four explicit border panels (Top/Left/Right/Bottom) each docked, with Bottom added LAST to guarantee it claims its space
   - BackColor border technique: parent BackColor = border color, Padding reveals it (used for bottom strip)
   - Make3DPanel: Dock=Left fixed-width outer panel with 4 border panels + Dock=Fill content
   - Per-row-count height: naturalH = (ROW_H+6) + rowCount*ROW_STRIDE + 4 + 2*B; fitsInView = naturalH ≤ TAB_MAX_H (850)
   - Dictionary<string, Label> for live value label lookup
   - Thread-safe UpdateValue() using BeginInvoke
   - Serial port async WriteFile with OVERLAPPED structure
   - ICD telemetry variable mapping (177 variables across 8 tabs)

   Make3DPanel (definitive version):
   ```csharp
   private Panel Make3DPanel(Control content, int rowCount, bool forceDockLeft = false)
   {
       const int B   = 3;
       Color     CLR = Color.FromArgb(200, 200, 200);
       int contentH    = (ROW_H + 6) + rowCount * ROW_STRIDE + 4;
       int naturalH    = contentH + 2 * B;
       bool fitsInView = !forceDockLeft && (naturalH <= TAB_MAX_H);
       var outer = new Panel { BackColor = Color.FromArgb(12, 12, 12) };
       if (fitsInView)
       {
           outer.Location = new Point(0, 0);
           outer.Size     = new Size(TAB_ROW_W + 2 * B, naturalH);
           outer.Anchor   = AnchorStyles.Top | AnchorStyles.Left;
       }
       else
       {
           outer.Dock  = DockStyle.Left;
           outer.Width = TAB_ROW_W + 2 * B;
       }
       content.Dock = DockStyle.Fill;
       outer.Controls.Add(content);
       outer.Controls.Add(new Panel { Dock = DockStyle.Top,    Height = B, BackColor = CLR });
       outer.Controls.Add(new Panel { Dock = DockStyle.Left,   Width  = B, BackColor = CLR });
       outer.Controls.Add(new Panel { Dock = DockStyle.Right,  Width  = B, BackColor = CLR });
       outer.Controls.Add(new Panel { Dock = DockStyle.Bottom, Height = B, BackColor = CLR });
       return outer;
   }
   ```

   BuildBottomStrip (definitive version):
   ```csharp
   private void BuildBottomStrip()
   {
       int halfW  = TAB_NW + 1 + TAB_VW;
       int stripW = 2 * halfW + 2;
       const int B   = 3;
       Color     CLR = Color.FromArgb(200, 200, 200);
       string[] leftNames  = { "Bot L1","Bot L2","Bot L3","Bot L4","Bot L5" };
       string[] rightNames = { "Bot R1","Bot R2","Bot R3","Bot R4","Bot R5" };
       this.Controls.Add(new Panel { Dock = DockStyle.Bottom, Height = 10, BackColor = BLACK });
       var pnlOuter = new Panel { Dock = DockStyle.Bottom, Height = BOT_H + 2*B, BackColor = BLACK };
       var pnlBox = new Panel {
           Location  = new Point(0, 0),
           Size      = new Size(stripW + 2*B, BOT_H + 2*B),
           BackColor = CLR, Padding = new Padding(B),
           Anchor    = AnchorStyles.Top | AnchorStyles.Left
       };
       var pnlInner = new Panel { Dock = DockStyle.Fill, BackColor = BLACK };
       var pnlLeft = BuildBottomHalf(leftNames, halfW);
       pnlLeft.Location = new Point(0, 0);
       pnlInner.Controls.Add(pnlLeft);
       var pnlRight = BuildBottomHalf(rightNames, halfW);
       pnlRight.Location = new Point(halfW + 2, 0);
       pnlInner.Controls.Add(pnlRight);
       pnlBox.Controls.Add(pnlInner);
       pnlOuter.Controls.Add(pnlBox);
       var statusBox = BuildStatusBox();
       statusBox.Location = new Point(stripW + 2*B + 4, 0);
       pnlOuter.Controls.Add(statusBox);
       this.Controls.Add(pnlOuter);
   }
   ```

   ```csharp
   {
   ```

   ```csharp
       for (int i = 0; i < varNames.Length; i++)
       {
           string vName = varNames[i];
           // NAME label uses vName instead of "Var XX"
           var valLbl = new Label { Text = "----", ... };
           _valueLabels[vName] = valLbl;  // stored for live updates
           row.Controls.Add(valLbl);
       }
   }
   ```

   Public UpdateValue API:
   ```csharp
   public void UpdateValue(string varName, float value)
   {
       if (this.IsDisposed) return;
       if (this.InvokeRequired)
       {
           this.BeginInvoke(new Action(() => UpdateValue(varName, value)));
           return;
       }
       if (_valueLabels.TryGetValue(varName, out Label lbl))
           lbl.Text = value.ToString("F2");
   }
   ```

**What changed:**

**PacketReceiver.cs:**

- Title bar now shows `RxBytes` and `CRCFail` counts on every 100 ms tick

**How to diagnose once running:**

| Title bar shows | Meaning |
|---|---|
| `RxBytes: 0` | Port open but nothing arriving — wrong COM port, cable, or hardware off |
| `RxBytes` growing, `CRCFail` growing | Data arriving but CRC mismatch — baud rate wrong, or transmitter uses different CRC seed |
| `RxBytes` growing, `CRCFail: 0` | Packets good but sync header (AA 55 DD) not being found |
| All normal | Should see live values updating |

The most common cause of `RxBytes: 0` is wrong COM port — double-check Device Manager while the hardware is connected.

   ```csharp
   // ... build content ...
   ```

**Two real issues I found in sgsim's encoder** (not your GCS, FYI):
1. `Throttle_pos` (packet byte 80): the encode line is commented out with `//NYI1` — the byte is never written, so it's garbage. Our decoder reads garbage for Throttle_pos.
2. `Slew_Rate_Alt_Com`: sgsim encodes it to `buff[28-29]` but only copies 28 bytes (indices 0–27) into the packet, so it's never transmitted. Packet byte 87 is always 0 (spare). Our `Slew_Rate_Alt_Com` field will always read 0.

Both are sgsim limitations, nothing to fix on the GCS side.

**Bottom line: the GCS decoder is correct and working.** To verify, set sgsim to a known heading/altitude and you'll see the GCS match it exactly.

```c
// Heading (buff[0-1] → pkt[62-63])
Limit = LimitVal(-0.0, 360.0, TelData.APGPSHeading);
tempd = (Limit - (-0))*182.0416666667;
tempi = (unsigned int) floor(tempd);
i2c.word = tempi;
HalfRate1buff[0] = i2c.byte[0];
HalfRate1buff[1] = i2c.byte[1];

// CAS (buff[10] → pkt[72])
Limit = LimitVal(-0.0, 100.0, TelData.CAS_m);
tempd = (Limit - (-0))*2.55;
HalfRate1buff[10] = (unsigned char) floor(tempd);

// Pressure Altitude / Hp (buff[15-16] → pkt[77-78])
Limit = LimitVal(-1000.0, 11000.0, TelData.pressalt);
tempd = (Limit - (-1000.0))*5.4612500000;
tempi = (unsigned int) floor(tempd);
i2c.word = tempi;
HalfRate1buff[15] = i2c.byte[0];
HalfRate1buff[16] = i2c.byte[1];
```

[654] CLAUDE
----------------------------------------
Four files changed. Here's what was done and why each change helps:

**PacketMonitorForm.cs** — added `if (!Visible || WindowState == FormWindowState.Minimized) return;` at the top of `OnTick`. The 200ms timer was running the full RTB color-render loop (hundreds of `Append()` calls per tick) even when the window was closed or minimized. Now it does nothing unless the window is actually open.

**PacketReceiver.cs** — three changes:
- Removed `Thread.Sleep(5)`. That was on the receive thread (not UI), so it didn't cause visual choppiness, but it added 5ms latency to every incoming data event.
- Added `private static readonly object _snapLock` that protects only the `PacketData[]/PacketReceived[]` arrays. The existing `_bufLock` held for the entire `ProcessBuffer()` call, which is too coarse for safe cross-thread reads.
- Added `TakeSnapshot()` which copies all 8 packet buffers under `_snapLock` and returns them together with the `received[]` flags. Now the UI thread works on its own copies and can never see a half-written packet.

**Form2.cs** — added `BeginUpdate()` / `EndUpdate()` using WM_SETREDRAW (the same P/Invoke already in PacketMonitorForm). Every `label.Text =` assignment triggers `Invalidate()` on that label. With 177 labels per tick, that's 177 queued paint messages. `BeginUpdate` suppresses painting for the entire form; `EndUpdate` restores it and fires one `Invalidate(true)` that covers all children.

**Form1.cs** — three changes:
- Replaces the 8 unguarded `PacketReceiver.PacketData[n]` reads with a single `TakeSnapshot()` call. Consistent, lock-safe.
- Decodes each packet only once. Previously the main display decoded packets 1–7, then Form2 re-decoded all of them — up to 14 `Decode()` calls per 100ms tick. Now it's one pass of up to 8 decodes, shared by both.
- Added `_form2.Visible` to the guard condition and wraps the entire Form2 push in `BeginUpdate()` / `EndUpdate()`.

Build in Visual Studio as usual (`Ctrl+Shift+B`). If it rejects the tuple deconstruction syntax (`var (snap, recv) = ...`) set `<LangVersion>7.3</LangVersion>` in the `.csproj` — though it should default to 7.3 on a VS 2017+ project targeting .NET 4.8.

- Added `TakeSnapshot()` public static method
```csharp
private static readonly object _snapLock = new object();

// In HandlePacket:
if (crcOk)
{
    lock (_snapLock)
    {
        Array.Copy(packet, PacketData[packetNum - 1], PACKET_LEN);
        PacketReceived[packetNum - 1] = true;
    }
    Console.WriteLine(...);
}

// New method:
public static (byte[][] data, bool[] received) TakeSnapshot()
{
    var data = new byte[TOTAL_PACKETS][];
    var recv = new bool[TOTAL_PACKETS];
    lock (_snapLock)
    {
        for (int i = 0; i < TOTAL_PACKETS; i++)
        {
            data[i] = new byte[PACKET_LEN];
            Array.Copy(PacketData[i], data[i], PACKET_LEN);
            recv[i] = PacketReceived[i];
        }
    }
    return (data, recv);
}
```

```csharp
private static extern int SendMessage(IntPtr hWnd, int msg, bool wParam, int lParam);
private const int WM_SETREDRAW = 11;

public void BeginUpdate()
{
    if (IsHandleCreated)
        SendMessage(Handle, WM_SETREDRAW, false, 0);
}

public void EndUpdate()
{
    if (IsHandleCreated)
    {
        SendMessage(Handle, WM_SETREDRAW, true, 0);
        Invalidate(true);
    }
```
```csharp
}
```

**C:\Users\uzama\source\repos\GCS_240626\TelemetryDecoder.cs** — READ ONLY (no changes)
- `U()` helper function confirmed correct:
```csharp
private static double U(byte[] p, int offset, int n, double minEng, double maxEng)
{
    ulong raw = 0;
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++)
        raw |= (ulong)p[offset + i] << (8 * i);  // little-endian: LSB at lowest address
    double maxRaw = (1UL << (n * 8)) - 1;
    return raw / maxRaw * (maxEng - minEng) + minEng;
}
```
- All field decode calls verified correct against ICD

[683] CLAUDE
----------------------------------------
Root cause is clear. The "Real time" property defaults to **"No"** — so `SimData.RealTime = 0` and the simulation runs flat-out. Each iteration takes ~16ms of CPU time, giving 10/16 = **62.5% of real-time speed**.

Two separate problems need fixing in SGMain.cpp:

**Problem 1:** "Real time" = No → no pacing at all → runs at CPU speed (~62.5% realtime)  
**Problem 2:** If you set "Real time" = Yes, the wait loop calls `Sleep(5)` — on Windows with default 15.6ms timer resolution, that sleeps ~15.6ms instead of 5ms, overshooting the 10ms target and *still* giving ~64% real time

The fix is to add `timeBeginPeriod(1)` (1ms timer resolution) and change `Sleep(5)` → `Sleep(1)`:

[684] CLAUDE
----------------------------------------
Now I have everything. The fix requires two changes to SGMain.cpp:

1. `timeBeginPeriod(1)` — sets Windows timer to 1ms resolution so `Sleep()` is accurate
2. `Sleep(5)` → `Sleep(1)` — so the pacing loop sleeps in 1ms increments instead of the Windows default ~15.6ms tick

[685] CLAUDE
----------------------------------------
Now fix the `Sleep(5)` in the pacing loop:

[686] CLAUDE
----------------------------------------
Three changes to **SGMain.cpp**:

1. Added `#include <mmsystem.h>` + `#pragma comment(lib, "winmm.lib")` — links the Windows multimedia timer API.

2. `timeBeginPeriod(1)` before `while(Go)` — sets the OS timer resolution to 1 ms globally for this process. Without this, `Sleep(N)` rounds up to the nearest 15.6 ms tick, which is why a `Sleep(5)` was actually sleeping ~15.6 ms and the simulation was running at 62.5% speed.

3. `Sleep(5)` → `Sleep(1)`, threshold changed to `SimDelta*1000 - 1` — the loop now sleeps 1 ms at a time, busy-spinning only for the last 1 ms, giving accurate 10 ms pacing instead of ~16 ms.

4. `timeEndPeriod(1)` after the loop — restores the default timer resolution on exit (good practice system-wide).

**Also required:** in the sgsim Properties panel, set **"Real time" = "Yes"** before running. The pacing loop only activates when `SimData.RealTime == 1`. Without that, the simulation still runs flat-out. Then rebuild sgsim in Visual Studio.

[693] CLAUDE
----------------------------------------
Three fixes applied:

**Fix 1 (PacketReceiver.cs):** Silenced `Console.WriteLine` in the hot receive path. Every stored packet was logging — at 8 packets per sgsim cycle, that's hundreds of console writes per second, each one blocking the receive thread with a kernel lock while data piles up in the serial buffer.

**Fix 2 (Form1.cs):** Timer interval `100 ms → 50 ms`. Display now refreshes at 20 Hz instead of 10 Hz, halving the worst-case display lag from 100 ms to 50 ms.

**Fix 3 (Form1.cs):** `_combined.Refresh()` → `_combined.Invalidate()`. `Refresh()` is a synchronous blocking paint — it stalls `UpdateDisplay` until the PFD finishes drawing with AntiAlias. `Invalidate()` just marks the region dirty and returns immediately; the actual paint happens in the next message pump cycle, off the critical path.

Rebuild and you should see noticeably snappier display response.

[694] USER
----------------------------------------
if i increase the baud rates, would it help to increase the speed

[695] CLAUDE
----------------------------------------
No — for two reasons:

**1. Virtual COM pair ignores baud rate for actual transfer speed.** COM24↔COM9 is a software loopback in the kernel. Data moves through shared memory, not through a UART. The baud rate setting is honored in the API but has no effect on how fast bytes get from sgsim to the GCS — it arrives almost instantly regardless of what baud rate is configured on both ends.

**2. Even on a real serial link, 115200 is not the bottleneck.** If sgsim sends one 164-byte packet per autopilot cycle at 50 Hz:

```
164 bytes × 10 bits × 50 Hz = 82,000 bits/sec
```

115200 baud carries 115,200 bits/sec — so the link is only at **71% utilisation**. There's already headroom. The display timer (now 50 ms) is the dominant latency, not transmission time.

The fixes already applied (removing `Console.WriteLine`, 50 ms timer, `Invalidate()`) address the real bottlenecks. The baud rate is fine as-is.

```csharp
private static void DecodeHalfRate_Frame1(byte[] p, TelemetryData d)
{
    d.Heading           = U(p,  72, 2,     0,    360);
    d.Latitude          = U(p,  74, 4,   -90,     90);
    d.Longitude         = U(p,  78, 4,  -180,    180);
    d.CAS               = U(p,  82, 1,     0,    100);
    d.PS                = U(p,  83, 2, 22600, 108000);
    d.PD                = U(p,  85, 1,     0,   6400);
    d.TAS               = U(p,  86, 1,     0,    100);
    d.Hp                = U(p,  87, 2, -1000,  11000);
    d.Throttle_com      = U(p,  89, 1,     0,      1);
    d.Throttle_pos      = U(p,  90, 1,     0,      1);
    d.Radar_Alt         = U(p,  91, 2,     0,    100);

    d.CAS_Com           = U(p,  95, 1,     0,    100);
    d.Alt_Com           = U(p,  96, 1,     0,  11000);

    d.AGL               = U(p,  98, 2,     0,   1000);
    d.Slew_Rate_Alt_Com = U(p, 100, 2,     0,  11000); // 2 B in sgsim
}
```
